Public Telegram 82

To All Newspaper Offices in Hailar: A telegram was recently sent to the League of Nations, which reads as follows: "Entrusted by representatives of the people of various localities in the Northeast and supported by the generals of various armies, I, the Commander-in-Chief and Deputy Commander-in-Chief, assumed office as the Commander-in-Chief and Deputy Commander-in-Chief of the Northeast People's National Salvation Army on October 1, the 21st year of the Republic of China [1932] in Hailar. Before mobilizing troops to eliminate violence, I hereby present to all friendly nations around the world the treaty violations and atrocities committed by Japan over the years, as well as the true intentions of our 30 million people. Japan, with an aggressive ideology, forcibly occupied Northeast China, coerced and held Puyi hostage under the guise of popular opinion, and organized the puppet state of Manchukuo. More than a year has passed since then. The Chinese people have unanimously opposed it, and the entire territory is mired in endless chaos. Despite stationing heavy troops, Japan has no ability to maintain law and order, and it has intensified its regressive actions, committing arson, murder, rape, and plunder, all kinds of atrocities. In addition to adhering to reason and humanity, at least three-quarters of the residents of the Northeast can no longer make a living. This action damages the integrity of China's territory and sovereignty, violating Article 1 of the Nine-Power Treaty. Its failure to resolve disputes by peaceful means and its unauthorized use of force to disrupt peace violate Article 2 of the Kellogg-Briand Pact. It also infringes on the political independence of members of the League of Nations, disregarding advice and ignoring covenants, simultaneously violating Articles 10, 12, and 13 of the League of Nations Covenant. The international community has delayed until now and has been unable to restrain or stop Japan's atrocities. The Chinese people cannot but take urgent and effective self-defense measures. Recently, Japanese warlords have even brazenly concluded a treaty of recognition with the puppet state of Manchukuo, monopolizing the resources of the Northeast and blockading international commerce. The situation in East Asia is about to face a major crisis. The people of Northeast China can hardly endure it. Japan has forced the puppet state to promote popular self-determination, governance by benevolent rule, openness, equality, co-existence, and co-prosperity as deceptive slogans to blind the eyes and ears of the world and to cover up its forcible occupation of the Northeast, further laying the foundation for permanent secession. Our people have never recognized these coercive and despicable actions from beginning to end. As soldiers, we are obligated to save the country. Based on the wishes of our 30 million people, we are mobilizing troops to the east to overthrow Japan's barbaric militarism, determined to liberate all the people, restore the territory, eliminate the puppet state, and establish peace. All our friendly nations should know that Japanese warlords not only harm China but also threaten foreign nationals. If they are not driven out, China and foreign countries will all feel threatened. Since the Japanese aggressive army and the Chinese bandit groups it has bought over are clearly unable to maintain the security of various cities, the Northeast is, from this day forward, only under the responsible authority of our People's National Salvation Army. All Chinese and foreign residents will be protected wherever our army goes. Anyone who obstructs our army's actions or acts as a tool of Japanese aggression, regardless of nationality, will not be protected. Furthermore, the Japanese people have not benefited from the Northeast Incident, but their burdens have increased, their economy has been plunged into panic, and unemployment is increasing day by day. They are also under oppression. In this case, our army is directly seeking freedom for the Chinese nation and indirectly removing tyranny for the Japanese people, as well as seeking lasting peace for all the nations of the world, so that the true intentions of our 30 million people in the Northeast can be revealed to the world and will not be slandered by violence. We also hope to unite with all those who are aware and striving for liberation to form a united front, attacking from both the front and the rear. This is a battle for the survival of the people of East Asia, and it is hereby proclaimed to the world. Respectfully submitted, Commander-in-Chief of the Northeast People's National Salvation Army Su Bingwen, Deputy Commander-in-Chief Zhang Dianjiu, respectfully sent and sealed."

Japanese Arbitrarily Incorporate 83

Yanbian into Korean Territory

Establish Jiantao Administrative District

Appoint Korean as Chief

Dalian Dispatch: The counties of Hunchun, Yanji, and Longjingcun in Jilin Province are located on the border between China and Korea and are adjacent to each other. In recent years, the number of Koreans coming to Yanbian to cultivate land has increased. Currently, the Korean population in Yanbian and other counties exceeds 400,000, while the Chinese population is less than three-tenths of the Korean population. In March of this year, the puppet state borrowed a large sum of 20 million yuan from Japan, on the condition that Yanbian be ceded. As a result, the Japanese seized all rights in Yanbian and began to incorporate Hunchun, Yanji, and Longjingcun into Korean territory, assigning them to an administrative district under the control of the Korean Governor-General's Office. In May of this year, the Governor-General dispatched Tanaka, the chief of the foreign affairs section, to reside in Yanji to prepare for the establishment of the so-called Jiantao Special Administrative District. All investigations, organizations, and police deployments are now in place. On the 8th of this month, Tanaka returned to Korea to report on his mission. The Japanese are now planning to relocate a large number of Korean people to eastern Jilin, adopting the so-called "collective immigration policy." The Korean Governor-General's Office has decided to appoint a Korean as the administrative chief of the Jiantao Special District. The Japanese's arbitrary seizure of our territory is clearly a violation of the integrity of our country's territory, and our diplomatic authorities should promptly protest it. (October 12th)

China Eastern Railway

The Honor of the Anti-Government Army 84

Foreigners Praise Them as Very Polite

Japanese Telegram Also Confirms No Killings or Looting

Intent Solely to Resist the Puppet State of Manchukuo

A Harbin dispatch from the North China Daily News on October 2nd states: "Every time newspapers announce that Japanese troops have cleared out bandits in a certain area, new incidents follow, worsening the situation and even making it far worse than before. Since April 26th, the eastern section of the Chinese Eastern Railway has been closed to traffic, with only occasional trains running between Harbin and a section of the border, and never directly to Vladivostok. The Chinese soldiers' strategy of dispersing and ambushing is exhausting the Japanese troops. The southern section of the Chinese Eastern Railway has also been damaged, but train services rarely stop except during floods, and the attacks by Chinese soldiers in this section are far less intense than in the eastern section. Currently, each train is accompanied by three armored cars, with half of the guards being Chinese and half being Japanese, to ensure safe passage according to the new regulations. Passenger trains only run during the day, while freight trains can still run unimpeded at night. According to train passengers, stray bullets occasionally hit the train, but there have been no incidents of tracks being destroyed. After the flood subsided, the western section of the railway reopened, much to the relief of the business community, who hoped that transportation to Europe could be restored. However, within a few days, alarms came from Manchouli and Hailar, stating that the railway protection troops had rebelled, detaining all Chinese, Japanese, and Russian personnel related to the puppet Manchukuo government. This uprising was incredibly swift and astonishing. In less than a day, the railway from Manchouli to Fularji was entirely in the hands of the anti-government army. The puppet Manchukuo flags at all stations were torn down and replaced with old flags. Telegraph and telephone lines were cut. The purpose of this new movement was initially unknown, but it was later learned that it was aimed at resisting the puppet Manchukuo state. The anti-government army apparently had no conflict with the railway authorities, as trains were still able to pass. Yesterday morning, several foreigners took the train south to this city. According to them, the soldiers treated passengers very politely, but searches were very strict to prevent personnel related to the puppet Manchukuo state from blending in. The rumors of Chinese soldiers arbitrarily killing Japanese residents have also been denied. One passenger said that he personally saw the Japanese consul in Manchouli walking down the street. Although there were some robbery cases, they were very few. Overall, everyone agreed that the riot in Manchouli was quelled within two hours. Yesterday morning, news came from Harbin that the Chinese army was currently besieging Qiqihar. The general manager of the Chinese Eastern Railway, Lutkevich, ordered the trains from Harbin to Qiqihar to be temporarily suspended pending further orders because the telegraph and telephone lines to Qiqihar were suddenly cut. As a result, the western section of the railway has now been suspended again. The Japanese military mission claimed this morning that ordinary Japanese residents in Manchouli, Hailar, and Qiqihar were not harmed. This can correct the various wild tales of Chinese soldiers wantonly killing and looting reported in the local Russian newspapers. This matter has also been confirmed by a special radio telegram from the Toho News Agency. From this, it can be seen that the purpose of the Chinese soldiers' uprising is not to harm civilians, but to have other great ambitions."

Great Awakening in Fujian Business Circles 85

Iron Blood Group Punishes Treacherous Merchants

Inferior Goods Burned at the Sports Field

A Fuzhou dispatch: "Inferior goods from a certain country are extremely prevalent in Fuzhou. Recently, enthusiastic people from society have organized the National Salvation Iron Blood Group, dedicated to dealing with treacherous merchants by force. The methods are divided into three steps: first warning, second ear cutting, and third assassination. Since the establishment of the group, the ears of Zhang Kangjian, the owner of Xiexing Cloth Shop, and Liu Yin, the owner of Tianji Cloth Shop, have been cut off, and Liu Yinghui, a foreign cloth broker, has been killed. On the evening of the eighth of this month, at around 8 p.m., Zhang Qiufan, the manager of the Guangdong Coal Mine in the Hexi Street area near the Pacification Commissioner's Office, was shot dead with a pistol. His crime was written in white powder on the wall of his house, accusing him of colluding with Taiwanese people, specializing in selling inferior coal and foreign cloth and opium, and ignoring warnings. The business community was greatly shocked. On the afternoon of the ninth, an emergency meeting of various merchant guilds was convened at the Chamber of Commerce, resolving to have each guild's shop automatically carry all the inferior goods from a certain country stored by them to the public sports field for burning at 12 noon on Double Ten Day, to show their determination to never buy or sell them again. If any more goods from a certain country are found afterward, they will be considered to be undermining the patriotic front and regarded as public enemies, and society will have to deal with them with the most severe means of dealing with enemies. On this day, over a thousand dan of inferior goods from a certain country were carried from various shops to the sports field for burning, piled up like a mountain. The smoke and flames filled the sky, and tens of thousands of spectators clapped and cheered. Each shop also posted slogans at the entrance stating that the inferior goods in their shop had been thoroughly cleared out and welcoming patriotic comrades to come inside for inspection, which shows the great upsurge of popular sentiment in Fujian Province." (October 10th)

Amended and Passed by the Legislative Yuan

Banknote Issuance Tax Law 86

The amended Banknote Issuance Tax Law, after being discussed by the Legislative Yuan last week and handed over to the Finance Committee to be jointly reviewed with the Economic Committee, was immediately discussed at a joint meeting of the two committees. Representatives from the Ministry of Finance attended to explain the law, and the case was amended and passed with the following suggestions: (1) Since banks must first obtain the government's special permission to issue banknotes before paying the banknote issuance tax to the government, the government should formulate a Banknote Issuance Law to provide a basis for granting special permission to banks to issue banknotes, and then draft a Banknote Issuance Tax Law based on the Banknote Issuance Law. Otherwise, banks that have obtained special permission from the government to issue banknotes will not have precise regulations on their issuance volume and procedures, which is inconsistent with the main objective of reorganizing finance and banking. Therefore, it is suggested that this Yuan recommend that the Central Political Council instruct the Ministry of Finance to quickly draft a Banknote Issuance Law and submit it to this Yuan for review. (2) The power to concentrate banknote issuance can only be achieved with a well-organized central bank. Item 5 of the plan to improve the financial system passed by the First Plenary Session of the Fourth National Congress states: "The central bank should be detached from the direct command of the Ministry of Finance to maintain its independent financial status. The president and vice president should be appointed from those with banking knowledge and experience, and should not advance or retreat with financial personnel, nor should they be concurrently held by government personnel." This is to ensure the soundness of the central bank's organization. Therefore, it is proposed that this Yuan recommend that the Central Political Council, based on the resolution of the Fourth National Congress, decide on the principle of instructing the Ministry of Finance to quickly draft a Central Bank Law as the fundamental measure for unifying banknotes in the future. It was submitted to the 206th meeting of the Legislative Yuan today (the 15th) for discussion, and it was resolved to pass the amended draft after review. The amended draft is as follows: Amended Banknote Issuance Tax Law (Article 1) Designated banks specially permitted by the National Government to issue banknotes shall pay banknote issuance tax in accordance with this law. (Article 2) The banknote issuance tax shall be paid uniformly, regardless of silver dollar notes or subsidiary coin notes. The aforementioned subsidiary coin notes shall be calculated at ten jiao to one yuan. (Article 3) Banks issuing banknotes shall have full reserve funds, with at least 60% as cash reserves and the remainder as guarantee reserves. The cash reserve portion shall be exempt from issuance tax. (Article 4) Banks issuing banknotes shall truthfully report the amount issued and the amount of cash and guarantee reserves separately in accordance with the monthly report form prescribed by the Ministry of Finance. The aforementioned reported amounts shall be registered separately by the Ministry of Finance on a monthly basis, and after one year, they shall be calculated based on the average of twelve months. (Article 5) The banknote issuance tax rate shall be set at 1.25% based on the actual amount of guarantee reserves. (Article 6) The banknote issuance tax shall be collected once at the beginning of each fiscal year based on the average of the previous year. (Article 7) Banks that are required to pay the banknote issuance tax shall, after receiving the collection notice from the Ministry of Finance, pay the tax to the local central bank within ten days for collection by their respective head offices, obtain a receipt, and report it to the Ministry of Finance for verification. (Article 8) If a bank fails to pay the banknote issuance tax in accordance with this law, the Ministry of Finance may, with approval, revoke its special issuance right. (Article 9) If the Ministry of Finance deems that the amount reported by a bank in accordance with Article 4 is not accurate, it may send personnel to inspect the issuance accounts and reserve fund accounts. If there is indeed concealment or underreporting, in addition to being ordered to pay the issuance tax, a fine of between 500 yuan and 3,000 yuan shall also be imposed. (Article 10) Banks issuing banknotes shall also pay the taxes due for the banknotes used by other banks, but they may recover the tax from the banks using the banknotes. (Article 11) This law shall take effect from the date of promulgation."

Request for Revision by the Navy Department

Regulations on Maritime Capture and Other Laws 87

The Navy Department stated that the three types of naval regulations: Maritime Capture Regulations, Capture Review Office Regulations, and Rules for the Custody of Captured Objects by Naval Offices, were all promulgated separately in 1917. However, they have been in effect for a long time, and many of the wordings are no longer applicable today. However, these regulations are all related to international justice and should not be revised directly by the ministry. Therefore, a clean copy was prepared and submitted to the Executive Yuan to be forwarded to the Legislative Yuan for revision and promulgation separately for implementation. The Executive Yuan forwarded it to the Military Affairs Commission for review, and the Military Affairs Commission replied, stating that since these regulations are related to international justice, the esteemed Yuan is requested to consult with the Legislative Yuan for revision and

Page 10

promulgation to demonstrate prudence. The Executive Yuan has already submitted the original documents to the Legislative Yuan for review at the meeting on the 15th.

Chen Guohui's Troops Have Been Resolved 88

Remaining Troops Fleeing Towards Dehua

A Fuzhou dispatch: "After Chen Guohui, the brigade commander of the First Mixed Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army, was detained by the Pacification Commissioner's Office, Chen's five regiments, totaling more than 7,000 men, concentrated in Xianyou County, under the command of Chen Peiyu, the regimental commander of the Second Regiment, preparing to resist. The Pacification Commissioner's Office dispatched two regiments of Tan Qixiu's Provincial Supplementary Brigade to Yongtai County for defense. Zhang Yan, the deputy division commander of the 61st Division stationed in Quanzhou, led three regiments of Zhang Li's brigade and one regiment of the 60th Division stationed in Zhangzhou to Yongchun and Hui'an counties for defense, encircling them from three sides and ordering them to surrender. Cai Tingkai also personally went to Quanzhou to command. On the third, firing began in the Shuikou Fengding area of Yongchun. Chen's troops, relying on their familiarity with the terrain, stubbornly resisted, with Peng Tang, the regimental commander of the First Regiment, supervising the battle. Zhang's brigade used artillery bombardment. On the fourth, Peng Tang was killed in action by artillery fire, and the bandits collapsed. The 19th Route Army took the opportunity to pursue, and Chen's troops suffered more than a thousand casualties and captures, with more than 2,000 rifles and more than ten machine guns seized. The remaining troops retreating into Xianyou were intercepted by the militia and more than 1,000 rifles were seized. Upon hearing the news, the rear echelon knew that the situation was over. On the morning of the fifth, they retreated from Xixiang to Xingtai Li, fleeing towards Dehua, because that area has high mountains and steep terrain, and for more than ten years, it has been the base for bandits in the four counties of Xian, Yong, and De. On the afternoon of the fifth, Zhang Yan led troops from Nanxiang to enter Xiancheng. Merchants set off firecrackers to welcome them. Zhang immediately dispatched Zhang Li's brigade to advance towards the north of Xianyou to search for bandit traces. He stayed overnight and returned to Quanzhou, handing over local security to Chen Tong's regiment of Chen Wei'yuan's Third Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army. However, the people of Xianyou and Putian counties believe that Chen Wei'yuan's troops are also composed of bandits. When they were stationed in Xianyou before, they imposed exorbitant taxes and levies, which were no less than Chen Guohui's. The recent burning and killing of DongsHa village in Putian County is one example. They specifically elected representatives to go to Fuzhou and Zhangzhou to request Jiang and Cai to punish He Xianzhu, the deputy brigade commander of the Third Brigade, and to completely resolve the troops under his command, together with Chen Guohui's troops, in order to permanently relieve the suffering of the people of Xinghua."

Attached is the telegram from Zhang Yan and Zhang Li to Jiang and Cai reporting the defeat of Chen's troops: "Director and Commander-in-Chief, We received the order to lead our troops to Xianyou to monitor Chen's troops. Our army arrived at Motou Creek and followed orders to avoid conflict, hoping to allow them to surrender peacefully without alarming the neighborhood. However, Chen's troops had divided wills, and the rebellious ones were plotting. When Peng Tang saw us approaching, he opened fire first. We still strongly suppressed our soldiers and repeatedly enlightened them, encouraging them to strive forward. After two fierce battles at Fengding and Shuikou, the bandits scattered like birds and beasts, abandoning their weapons and baggage. Those injured and killed filled the pits and valleys. Our army, without fear of hardship, followed and pursued urgently, and captured more than 1,000 rifles and eight machine guns. The number of captives and those killed in battle totaled more than 1,000. The bandit Peng Tang was killed on the battlefield. Another unit was intercepted by the militia and also had more than 1,000 rifles seized. The rest scattered in four directions and are now being recruited and captured. The weapons seized by the militia have been ordered to be handed over to our troops in full for rewards. This is the general situation of Chen's troops' resistance and defeat. I, Yan, will return to Quanzhou to handle the aftermath of Huian County, and I, Li, will stay in Xianyou to handle the unfinished business of suppression and pacification. We humbly submit this telegram, Yan and Li, respectfully knocking. Good afternoon." (October 11th)

Songjiang 89

Record of the Interrogation of the "Little Taibao" Murder Case: Thirteen years ago, the Zhang Dongfu family in Baojia Bridge, west of the city, suffered the brutal murder of three women by Li Ting and others, a scene that is still vivid in memory. Only one murderer, Shen Aqin, was captured in the case, and after being interrogated by the county government, was executed by firing squad. This spring, the criminal sneaked back to Shanghai and committed another murder case in the French Concession's Great World, was apprehended, and sentenced to eight years in prison by the Second Special District Court. The county court of this county dispatched police to escort him back to Songjiang for investigation. Today, Prosecutor Zhu opened the court for investigation, and witnesses Zhang Ren and others were summoned to testify. Other witnesses, Lin Feng, A Mei, Zhao Qinglong, etc., could not be summoned because their addresses were unknown. The court ordered Zhang Ren to find them and bring them to court. Suzhou 90

A Fierce Battle Between Police and Bandits in Dongzhu: Lake bandits in Taihu Lake appear and disappear unpredictably. They are difficult to eliminate, and suppressing one leads to the rise of another. Although the military and police authorities have repeatedly suppressed them severely, it only treats the symptoms. Addressing the root causes requires huge expenses, and for thousands of years, it has not been realized. At 8 a.m. on the 13th of this month, Wang Zhaomin, the leader of the first squad of the second squadron of the county police stationed in Fanzhouzhuang, was ordered to patrol along the lake with twelve members of the second squadron of the 14th water police team. On the way, they received a report from villagers that thirty to forty lake bandits from Pudong were sailing towards Qingpu on three large boats and one small boat. The water police immediately led the way, trying to intercept them. At about 11 a.m., they arrived at Dongzhu Village, which belongs to Wujiang County, about two li from the border between Qingpu and Kunshan. They learned that the bandit boats were docked at Dongtan, so they rushed to the squad. They first encountered a small bandit boat with only hostages on board. They said that all the bandits were having lunch in a small temple on the shore. The water police landed and launched an encircling attack. The bandits also resisted with weapons. The water police were outnumbered and retreated to the boat, allowing the bandits to rush out and board the boat. At this time, the police arrived and took the lead, temporarily mixing and dividing into three teams, surrounding and attacking from the left, right, and center. The bandits still resisted stubbornly and also divided into three routes to meet the attack, fighting and retreating repeatedly. The fierce battle lasted until 1 p.m., with two bandits killed and about five or six wounded. The bandits could not hold out and fled towards Yushan Lake with their dead and wounded. In this battle, there were no casualties on the police side. They seized a small boat numbered Qingpu He 8890 and rescued three hostages: Li Shaoyun, Zhu Ma's, and Ren Falin. On the 15th, they were escorted to the third district of the water police here by the 14th team and notified the families of those kidnapped to come to Suzhou to claim them.

Wuxi 91

Hopes for Resolution of the Silk Factory Strike: The general strike of silk factories in the county has lasted for eight days, and the situation is becoming increasingly serious. The arrival of He Yushu, director of the Industry Bureau, Li Mingyang, director of the Provincial Security Department, and Zhang Gongren, member of the Provincial Party Committee, the serious situation seems to have hopes for development. Yesterday, the Silk Factory Industry Association decided to have the seriously injured female workers go to court to verify their injuries and request legal aid due to the police's assault on the female workers. At the same time, they submitted a report to the county government requesting an investigation into the police officers who committed the violence. At 2 p.m., the association held another representative conference, resolving: 1. The agreed-upon points of dispute must be handled according to the original agreement before they can be accepted. 2. A representative conference will be held again on the 16th after the mediation meeting on the 15th. 3. The fault for this strike lies with the capitalists, and the wages during the strike period should be paid by the capitalists. 4. All members of the association and representatives attending from various factories should not be allowed to resign or publish their resignations because they deem the handling of matters difficult. At about 4 p.m., four seriously injured female workers, Zeng Fumei, Cao Afeng, Zhu Gendi, and Fu Sanmei, went to the county court to verify their injuries. Chief Zhou opened the court, ordered the clerks to verify the injuries, and ordered them to be sent back for review. At 8:04 p.m., He Yushu, Li Mingyang, Zhang Gongren, Jiang Nanchun, Yi Tingjian, and others, a group of six people, arrived in Wuxi on the fourth special express train going south. They immediately inquired in detail from County Magistrate Chen about the strike process. According to He, the mediation steps for the Wuxi strike have been determined. The first step is to separately summon the capitalists and workers one after another on the afternoon of the 15th to hold separate talks, inquire in detail about the factory's conclusions on the strike, and the current situation of the capitalists and the demands of the workers. The second step is to formulate a mediation plan that can be accepted by both parties based on the results of the separate talks and the possibilities of the facts and environment. The third step is to convene a joint mediation meeting of labor and capital to announce the formulated mediation plan and persuade both parties to accept it. According to Li Mingyang, when he first saw the report about the Wuxi strike, he suspected that there were reactionaries and other complex backgrounds behind the scenes. After sending personnel to Wuxi for investigation, he learned that the cause of the strike was very simple and there was no complex background, so he had changed his policy and decided to resolve it through peaceful means. As for sending troops to Wuxi, it was entirely to maintain local security. According to Zhang Gongren, the strike can be divided into two parts: legal and factual. From a legal point of view, the workers' sudden strike was a big mistake, but their insistence on the old agreement was not unreasonable. However, from a factual point of view, there were as many as 50 silk factories in Wuxi in the past, and there are still 24 that are closed, which shows that the situation of the capitalists is also difficult. The provincial government's handling of the strike should replace the old agreement under the principle of taking into account the interests of both labor and capital, but work must be resumed first before negotiations can be held. The two points that the workers did not make legal demands and suddenly went on strike, and that the treatment of each factory was different and there were no standards, are regrettable to me. At about 12 p.m., five companies of the first battalion of the third regiment of the Provincial Security Force, led by Regiment Commander Li Changjiang and Battalion Commander Yang Wei, arrived in Wuxi by train and were stationed in Nan Shui Xian Temple, Zhang Yuan Temple, and Xi Shui Xian Temple. Today, they have sent teams to patrol inside and outside the city. It is also heard that there is hope for resumption of work today (the 16th). It is also reported that He Yushu, director of the Industry Department, convened a meeting of capitalists at the Railway Hotel yesterday morning to exchange opinions. In the afternoon, the Silk Factory Industry Association held a general meeting, and He Yushu attended and urged the factories to start work. In the afternoon, the Silk Factory Workers' Union held a meeting, and Li Mingyang and Zhang Gongcheng went to give instructions. The workers on the spot requested the restoration of the labor-capital agreement. Li and others instructed the workers to submit it in writing. This morning, after considering the opinions of both labor and capital, a mediation plan has been determined. A mediation meeting will be held in the afternoon, and work will officially resume tomorrow.

The Jingzi Port Police and Bandits Open Fire: Recently, lake bandits have become rampant again. Shen Gaozhen, the commander of the second and third water police districts, ordered each team to unite and block them. The Zhaowu security ship and the Su Er patrol ship of the second district were towing three patrol boats and patrolling in Dianshan Lake when they encountered four bandit boats. As soon as the bandit boats saw the patrol ship, they sped away towards Xiaogang. The Zhaowu ship opened its engine and gave chase, but Xiaogang was too shallow to advance, allowing them to escape. At the same time, Captain Pei Xuan of the seventh team also personally led the patrol boat and patrolled to Jingzi Port when he encountered the bandits. The bandits resisted and opened fire. Soon, the bandits were overwhelmed and fled. As a result, they intercepted a bandit boat and rescued a female hostage surnamed Pan.

A Bizarre Murder Case in a Desolate Grave: Wu Jiquan, a resident of the Ten-Room Workshop at 5th Guangqin Road, Zhou Shanbang, outside the North Gate, had an argument with his concubine, Ms. Feng, the day before yesterday (the 14th) over a pawn ticket. Unexpectedly, yesterday morning, Ms. Feng suddenly hanged herself from a tree in a nearby desolate grave. However, observing the circumstances, it did not seem like a suicide. After Wu Jiquan learned about it, he reported it to the Sixth Branch of the Public Security Bureau in charge and instructed the map chief to report it to the county court, requesting them to send someone to investigate.

Notorious Escaped Bandit Li Chengguo Executed by Firing Squad: The notorious bandit Li Chengguo was arrested in January 1930 for robbing three families, including Wu Yuemao. The former County Magistrate Sun Zuji approved the report to the provincial government. On March 15th of that year, he was ordered to prepare for execution by firing squad. Unexpectedly, Li escaped from prison the day before and disappeared. The county issued a wanted notice. County Magistrate Chen approved the report to the provincial government and verified his identity at 10 a.m. yesterday (the 15th) before escorting him to the South School Field for execution by firing squad.

Nine Counties Jointly Suppress Lake Bandits: Wujin, Wuxi, Changzhou, Wuxian, Qingpu, Kunshan, Changshu, Yixing, Songjiang, and Jinshan counties formed a joint defense zone office in Wuxian for the sake of jointly protecting public security, and the county magistrates of each county served as commanders. At 10 a.m. yesterday, the office held its fifth joint defense meeting in Wuxi. More than ten people, including the county magistrates, public security bureau chiefs, water police district chiefs, and representatives from each county, attended. Zheng Jing, chief of the Wuxian Public Security Bureau, presided over the meeting and reported on the purpose of the meeting and the recent defense situation. The situation of each county's security was reported, followed by discussions on joint defense issues. With winter approaching, the future of security is extremely important, and teams should be allocated to jointly prevent and control. The resolutions of the previous meeting must be implemented, and the counties must jointly patrol. Next, the proposals of each county were discussed. Wuxian proposed that strict precautions should be taken against refugees entering the country, fearing that they would disrupt public security, and strict measures should be taken. Other counties proposed that the water and land police teams of each county along the lake must conscientiously suppress the lake bandits. There were many cases, but they were not announced due to defense matters. The meeting adjourned at 2 p.m. It was also heard that the next meeting will be held in Wujin.

Yangzhou 93

A Ministry Order Abolishes Salt Field Magistrates:

After the previous Ministry order to consolidate and reduce the number of salt fields in Lianghuai, there remained ten fields: Anfeng, Juegang Yu, Zhongxing, Xincao Yan, Wuyou, Jinan, Banpu, Zhongzheng, and Linxing. These were still managed by magistrates appointed by the Transportation Office. It is now heard that the Salt Affairs Department of the Ministry of Finance, for the sake of reorganizing salt affairs, has specially ordered the manager of the Banpu Inspection Sub-Office, who also serves as the Huai Bei Transportation Commissioner, Miao Qiujie, and the manager of the Yangzhou Inspection Sub-Office, who also serves as the Huai Nan Deputy Transportation Commissioner, Wang Zhanghu, to abolish all the salt field magistrates. All affairs of the various salt fields will be merged and handled by the respective inspection sub-offices.

Preventing Private Collection of Special Construction Tax:

Regarding the disputes between new and old merchants regarding the special construction tax in this county, it is now known that the county government yesterday received an order from the Construction Department. According to the report submitted by Gao Dian, a member of the Special Construction Tax Collection Committee, the old merchant Zhang Chuan (i.e., Zhang Zhaolin) is still obstructing tax collection and privately collecting the special tax, and has submitted evidence requesting an investigation. The county is now specially ordered to prevent this at any time and strictly prohibit the private collection of tax money. County Magistrate Yang has issued an order to the Public Security Bureau to comply.

New Zhenjiang Ferry Runs Aground in Fog:

The new Zhenjiang ferry of the Zhenyang Repair Company ran aground yesterday (the 14th) morning on its first trip from Zhenjiang to Yangzhou due to heavy fog. Passengers on board panicked. The company, upon receiving the news, consulted with the Zhenyi Pujii Ferry to transfer the passengers to the Yi Pier. The new Zhenjiang ferry was out of danger at twelve o'clock and safely arrived at Liuhe.

Rugao 94

Provincial Normal School Student Arrested and Sent to Tongzhou:

Shen Lu, a student at the Rugao Normal School in Jiangsu Province and a native of Libu District, was arrested at the school by police dispatched by the Rugao County Government on the night of the 10th in connection with the case of Lu Yangshan (a native of Rugao), a student at the Nantong Middle School of Jiangsu Province. On the morning of the 11th, he was sent to Nantong for investigation.

Three Bandits Apprehended in Xu Jiazhuang Robbery Case:

Regarding the robbery case at the home of Lu Rushan in Xu Jiazhuang, Fengli District, it is now heard that the district security corps has apprehended three bandits, including Chen Laibao, and is currently interrogating them.

Gaoyou 95

Wu Yizhuang Ji Family Robbery Case Cracked:

More than ten bandits suddenly came to the home of Ji Detai, a farmer in Wu Yizhuang, the seventh district of the county, and conducted a thorough search, robbing more than thirty piculs of indica rice, as well as silver dollars, clothing, and other items. The next morning, Ji glimpsed one of the robbers at a teahouse in Xiejiazhuang and immediately secretly reported it to the water patrol team stationed in the village, which apprehended the bandit. At the same time, Bai Daoshan, a village guard in Wu Yizhuang, suddenly posted a threatening letter to the doors of Wu Yangyuan, Wu Lianji, and Wu Lianji's three families. The letter stated that the three families were required to produce 600 yuan in foreign currency within seven days, otherwise they would be set on fire. As he was posting the letter, he was spotted by villagers, who immediately arrested Bai and sent him to the water patrol team. The team escorted the bandit and Bai, the village guard, to the city last night (the 12th) and transferred them to the county government for interrogation.

Pinghu 96

Large Quantities of Counterfeit Money Enter the Area:

The Frost's Descent solar term is approaching, which is traditionally the time for farmers to sell rice to pay rent. Unexpectedly, a large amount of counterfeit money has recently entered the area, causing countless victims. Recently, the farmer Zhang Wenhe sold an ox to a Mr. Mei for thirty-seven yuan, all in banknotes. The next day, Zhang went to pay rent and discovered that all the banknotes were counterfeit. He pursued Mr. Mei with an intermediary and had Mr. Mei arrested and placed in the custody of the Chu Jingfang neighborhood guard. He also wrote a petition requesting a thorough investigation. The source of this counterfeit money should not be difficult to ascertain.

Hefei 97

Tongcheng County Magistrate Killed in Bandit Den:

Tongcheng County Magistrate Yu Bohua was kidnapped by the bandit Zhang Daibi and taken to San Miao Temple. Initially, he was treated well, but he was ordered to write a letter asking his family to prepare a ransom of 30,000 yuan. Yu's father and son then sent someone to negotiate, explaining that they were poor. The amount was reduced from 20,000 to 10,000 yuan, but Yu's father only raised 7,000 yuan, which the bandits refused to accept, leading to a breakdown in negotiations. The Second Security Regiment under Ni Rongxian ordered a vigorous suppression, and the bandits fled over a hundred miles over several days, suffering many casualties. They took their anger out on Yu and killed him in revenge, according to a letter received.

New Compilation of the Army Second Division Beijing Communications Office Letter 98

To the esteemed editors of your newspaper:

Having read your publication's record of a Reuters Guangzhou dispatch of the 10th, which briefly stated that after the arrest of Chen Guohui, commander of the First Brigade of the Guangdong Provincial Defense Army, provincial military generals He Xianzhu and Lu Xingbang, among others, had made blatant expressions of opposition to the 19th Route Army, this is completely inconsistent with the facts. This division is a centrally-administered unit, and all actions are in accordance with central orders and the direct command of Zhuang, the Pacification Commissioner of Fujian. The Guangzhou Reuters dispatch is clearly due to outsiders' lack of understanding of the situation. Such spreading of misinformation affects military affairs and is of great importance. In addition to telegraphing the Military Affairs Committee Chairman Jiang to strictly prohibit this and issuing a public statement, we are writing to your newspaper to request a correction.

Respectfully,

Lu Xingbang, Commander of the New Compilation of the Army Second Division

Shanghai International Sports Meet - Day One

China Takes the Lead, England Close Behind 101

China Scores 24 Points, England 21 Points

The Championship Will Be a Fierce Competition Between the Two Countries

｜The Meet Breaks Five Chinese Men's and Women's Track and Field Records｜

｜Only Zhuang Mingzhen of Our Country Sets a New Women's Long Jump Record｜

The Third Shanghai International Sports Meet opened yesterday at the China Athletic Field with the majestic sound of military music. British athletes, with their outstanding performances, immediately scored twenty-one points in two events. Although China scored three more points, their hopes for the championship are slim. The British athletes performed exceptionally well in the short-distance races. It seems that the Chinese athletes cannot reach them. The preliminary rounds of the 100 meters, the top times in both groups, were 11.3 seconds, won by British athletes. In the 1,500 meters, British athletes took the top four places, with a time of 4 minutes and 21.4 seconds, a result never before seen in our country, except for an informal record of 4 minutes and 15 seconds incidentally set by Yu Xiwu. The British athlete Aker's time of 52.2 seconds in the 400 meters, the British athlete Warrell's time of 16.4 seconds in the high hurdles, and the American woman Burnett's high jump of 1.39 meters are all records never before seen in our country. Fortunately, Ms. Zhuang Mingzhen's long jump of 4.65 meters set a new record. The men's results this time are all remarkable. There will be fierce competition for the team championship between China and England. It is expected that both sides will go all out in today's finals.

The Opening Parade:

The competition was originally scheduled to begin at 1:45 PM, but the team parade did not begin until 2:00 PM. All the athletes and staff lined up behind the 100-meter starting line and paraded around the venue, led by the McInnes Military Band. Following the band were all the staff, then the women athletes from England, the United States, and China, followed by the male athletes from England, Russia, Japan, the United States, and China. The band played beautiful music, and the pace was steady. The whole venue erupted in thunderous applause, creating a magnificent scene. After circling the venue, they returned to the 100-meter starting line, and the competition began. It was already 2:15 PM.

The Audience Was Not Enthusiastic:

Yesterday's audience was only a little over a thousand before 3:00 PM. After 3:00 PM, the two sides of the north end of the stands were slightly crowded, with men, women, old, young, and people of all colors. It was estimated that there were about two thousand people, but it was not very enthusiastic. It is expected that today's program will be full of finals, and the interest will be even stronger, and the audience will definitely be lively.

China and England Compete for the Championship 104

If Chinese Athletes Do Not Strive, It Will Be Difficult to Have Hope

Before the International Sports Meet, everyone expected that China could steadily win the championship. In terms of predictions, they emphasized China and the United States. Little did they know that the American star Swank (the individual champion of the previous tournament) has now retired, and the performance of athletes such as Thompson Slaughter and Allard have greatly declined. Now that the United States has no special strengths, China's hope of retaining the championship seems greater. Who knew that England, which has always been weak, would show extraordinary performance this year, with great arrogance? Although the number of people is small, their performance is outstanding. Yesterday, they swept the top four places in the 1,500 meters and won the first place in the 400-meter relay. Their scores have reached twenty-one. Moreover, in the preliminary rounds of the 100 meters, 200 meters, and 400 meters, not only did they get the top scores, but their strength was also great, and there was much hope. Although China's total score was three points higher than England's yesterday, the situation is very dangerous. In addition, the Russian athletes' throwing army is also a major concern for China. Therefore, the championship of this competition will be contested by China and England. Even in individual events, China's score may not be less than England's. However, China's hope for the two relay races is extremely small. If England wins the 800-meter and 1,600-meter relay races, then China will be hopeless. An investigation revealed that most of the British athletes are from the Lancashire Regiment of the Shanghai Garrison. Since our country cannot win a place in the world arena, if we cannot steadily win the championship in the Shanghai International Sports Meet, what else can we say? Fortunately, I hope that our Chinese athletes will work hard to maintain the slight position of our country's track and field.

General Review of Yesterday's Track and Field (Liao) 106

Yesterday there were a total of five track and field events for men and women. There were three for men, and our athletes won two first places. There were two for women, and the United States and China shared the championship. The details are as follows:

Discus Final 107

Leng Peigen Lacks Experience

It was expected that there would be many discus throwers from the United States and Russia. Whether China could score points in the competition was considered beyond consideration. Therefore, at the time of registration, it was already calculated that Wang Jihuai, etc., would be reassigned to other events, and only Leng Peigen and Li Zier participated. Unexpectedly, the result of yesterday's competition was unexpected. The best result was only 34.89 meters, which was not as good as Leng Peigen's result in our country's preliminary round. Moreover, none of the Russian and American athletes who participated in the discus throwing had the correct throwing posture. They relied on their tall and strong physique. According to the score of 34.89 meters, it would not have been difficult for Leng Peigen to win the championship. Unfortunately, due to lack of experience, he often showed rapid breathing and panic at the time of throwing, resulting in a retreat to third place. There is one thing to offer to Mr. Leng: You have a naturally rich physique for throwing heavy objects. You should study the scientific methods of throwing heavy objects in detail. The speed of your discus throw is too fast when you start to turn, and your body is prone to lose balance. It should be modified. According to the scientific method of throwing the discus, the discus should be like a wave in a circle, starting from a downward curve and ending with an upward curve in the third wave. The discus should not be too fast on the downward curve. The speed should gradually increase on the upward curve in the second wave. If Mr. Leng can pay attention to this point, he will be able to enter the hall and enter the room in the future. I hope Mr. Leng will encourage him. The results of the four finalists are as follows:

First: Molotov (Russia) 34.89 meters

Second: Warwick (USA) 34.74 meters

Third: Leng Peigen (China) 33.80 meters

Fourth: Motovki (Russia) 33.65 meters

Long Jump Final 108

Wang Jihuai Unleashes Years of Resentment

Our country is full of long jumpers. Before the competition, it was known that it was our home field. However, the participants were still cautious and careful to prevent the story of the long jump at the International Sports Meet last year from happening again. According to the International Sports Meet last year, the long jump was entirely taken over by our country. At the last person, the national flag of our country was still hanging high on the flagpole in all directions, one, two, three, four, to show that our country had won a complete victory in this sport. Unexpectedly, in the last jump, the American Swank unexpectedly emerged as a dark horse, surpassing the scores of each person. From fifth, he won the final victory in one fell swoop. Wang Jihuai, who was originally the first, only had to advance to second place, and even the large silver cup could only be watched by Mr. Shi. It can be said that he had no words to say. Therefore, he was particularly careful in the competition this year. Unexpectedly, after six jumps, he hit a snag again. Wang Jihuai tied with the American Humphrey for first place with a score of 6.49 meters. It can be said that good things are hard to come by. However, according to the rules of track and field, there is no tie for first place. Each person must jump again to determine the order of the rankings according to the merits of one jump. Wang Jihuai's eyes were on fire. He used his life's strength to make a surprising jump. Sure enough, he lived up to the expectations of thousands of spectators in the stadium, overpowering Humphrey with a score of 6.69 meters. The resentment of the long jump failure last year has now been written off in one stroke. The results of the four are as follows:

First: Wang Jihuai (China) 6.49 meters

Second: Humphrey (USA) 6.49 meters

Third: Hao Chunde (China) 6.41 meters

Fourth: Sun Hupei (China) 6.31 meters

First and second are exceptional finals. Wang once jumped 6.67 meters, so he won first place, but the result is not counted.

High Jump Final 109

Ling Hongzhao Wins the Championship

Only nine people attended the high jump final. Among them, the postures of Ling Hongzhao, Gu Hu, Wu Jinqi of our country, and Guhe of Japan were more suitable. The rest of the postures were not suitable. Even the rolling style jumped by Li Lin of our country was not well researched, so it failed. As a result, although our country won the first, third and fourth seats, it can be called a complete victory, but Wu Jinqi was too disappointing. Not only could he not win the first place and create a new record, but he retreated to fourth place, defeated by Gu Yu and Wazi. The score was only 1.715 meters. Looking at Wu's legs, there was no strength at all. Compared to the Wu Jinqi of the past, it was like two different people. I wonder what the story is.

Women's High Jump 110

Burnett Retains the Championship

According to the order, there were only six women who joined the women's high jump. Later, with the permission of the referee, Misses Thomson and O'Kelly of England were temporarily allowed to join. Looking at each person's skills, there was no method to speak of. Last year's champion, American Ms. Burnett, relied on her naturally exquisite figure to retain the championship. The result was 1.39 meters, an improvement of 0.01 meters compared to her own result last year. This is an unprecedented record in our country. Although the British woman Thomson won the third place, it was not that the elasticity was not developed, but that she lacked training. According to Thomson's elasticity, it can be the crown of the whole body. If she can get proper training, then Burnett is far from her opponent. Ms. Zhuang Mingzhen of our country has a natural talent for jumping, but unfortunately, she has not mastered the speed of running and the rotation of the body when crossing the bar. In addition, the two women Li Baohui and Luo Yixue also lacked suitable methods. I hope they will work harder in the future.

The Situation of the Track and Field Duel 112

In yesterday's track and field finals, only the 1,500 meters and the men's and women's 400-meter relay races were dominated by British athletes, and our army was far inferior.

1,500 meters 113

British Athletes Take the Top Four Places

A total of thirteen people participated in the 1,500-meter final. Dong Jiaxie was the only athlete in China who had hope. After the start, the Chinese athletes were eliminated. Although Zhu Shaohua tried to take the lead and ranked second, he was also eliminated after one lap. Only the British and American athletes were competing for victory. After the second lap, the British Kennatai led by about two meters. The British Bessatto followed closely behind. The American child Sutton tried to chase, and the situation was good, but the pace seemed to be softer. By the last 200 meters, the rankings were largely determined. Bessatto took the lead and ran straight to the end, winning the championship by six or seven meters. The time was only 4 minutes and 21 seconds and 5/2, which is not as good as the official record in China. The British athletes continued to reach the finish line one after another, taking the top four places, which shocked the audience.

Women's 400-meter Relay 114

Chinese Women Strive to Achieve

Everyone thought that China would definitely fail in the women's 400-meter relay. Little did they know that as a result of the competition, the Chinese athletes took the lead all the way and ran straight to the end, winning the championship with a time of 58 seconds. The United States was second and England was third. The reason why the British and American athletes failed was that their talents were uneven and they lacked training. The order of the four Chinese athletes is as follows: (1) Qian Xingxiu, (2) Zhuang Mingzhen, (3) Chen Baoxiang, (4) Liu Jingfang.

400-meter Relay 115

England Overwhelms China

Although our country has short-distance running stars such as Wang Jihuai, Hao Chun, Peng Guangxin, and Fu Jincheng, they are no match for the British athletes. The British took the lead in the first leg. China was three or four meters behind. They competed with each other. The British athletes were mighty and powerful, and ran straight to the end, taking only 46.2/10 seconds. The second place was China, three or four meters behind. The third place was Russia, and the fourth place was Japan. The United States was eliminated.

Brief Description of the Preliminary Results 116

In the preliminary rounds of the 100 meters, China and England each took three places, but the first places in both groups were British athletes, and the times were also 11.3 seconds, one for Warrell and one for Hurst. The Chinese athletes were not as good. Wang Huai and Hao Chunde each took second place. It is difficult for our country to win the first and second places in today's final.

In the two groups of the 200 meters, Fu Jincheng of China was the best with 23.3 seconds, but Horry and Smith in the second group seemed to have not exerted their power. Hurst, who ran 11.3 seconds in the 100 meters, was overpowered by Fu. In today's final, if Fu Jincheng, the only remaining Chinese fruit, can maintain the result of 23.3 seconds, he should be able to win the championship.

The British Aker set a record of 52.2 seconds in the 400 meters, which has never been seen in our country. His posture and pace are excellent. The Chinese athletes cannot reach him. In today's final, China will at most only get the third or fourth place.

High Hurdles: This competition is considered to be China's special strength, and Chen Ling, who has a new national record, is even stronger. Little did they know that the British 100-meter runner Warrell also boasted to people with a score of 16.4 seconds, not letting Chen Ling and Li Men in front. Although Chen did not develop as much as possible yesterday, it is difficult for China to insure the championship in today's final. Xiao Dinghua kept the original time of 17 seconds, which is enough to compete with Warrell Chen Ling.

Intermediate Hurdles: In the preliminary rounds of this event, the three Chinese athletes Chen Ling, Tao Yingjie, and Guo Zhixin all had special performances. The American and British athletes were eliminated. Only the Russian Koguf and Brook of the open group were selected, which is not the enemy of China. The most characteristic result of the preliminary rounds was Chen Ling with 60.3 seconds. In today's final, all three Chinese athletes can be selected and can even take the top two places.

Jinan Decisively Defeats British Troops 120

7-1 Triumph Over Lancashire

With More Accurate Shots, It Could Have Been at Least a Dozen

| A Scene from the Group A Football Match |

Yesterday afternoon, the Jinan Football Team decisively defeated the British Lancashire team by a score of seven to one at the Recreation Ground football field. This marks Jinan's second consecutive major victory in the Group A league. Jinan had previously lost to Lancashire 2-3 in a friendly match, making this complete revenge, a resounding victory, particularly unexpected.

Perfect Coordination, Poor Shooting: Jinan's teamwork yesterday was truly flawless. The coordination of the five forwards was remarkably smooth, their incursions into the enemy's territory were exceptionally sharp. However, their shooting accuracy was lacking, with countless missed opportunities in front of the goal. Had their shooting been more precise, they could have scored over a dozen goals.

Yoyo Plays Fiercely Against the French Businessmen 124

| A 4-7 Defeat |

A Westerners' League Group A Match

Yesterday, the Yoyo Football Team played against the French Businessmen's team at the Baseball Field in a Westerners' League Group A match. After a fierce 90-minute battle, Yoyo lost 4-7. The referee was He Chunhui.

An Auspicious Start: This year marks Yoyo's first participation in Group A. The team comprises many veteran players, as well as several promising newcomers. Therefore, their performance has been quite commendable. The match against the French Businessmen's team was closely contested. However, their shooting accuracy was lacking, and they missed numerous opportunities. Otherwise, the outcome of the match would have been unpredictable. Yoyo started strong, with the entire team attacking. Mao Honggui sent a long pass, and Dong Xiaopei, displaying the skills he used to vie for supremacy in Nanyang with John, unleashed a powerful kick, breaking through the goal. However, in the blink of an eye, the opponents counterattacked, capitalizing on a free kick. Lei Ji'er seized the opportunity and scored. With each team scoring one goal, the game was tied after just five minutes.

The Goalkeeper's Liability: Liang Guanlian, who once made a name for himself in Shanghai, has been in retirement for a long time, and his skills have deteriorated. Most of the seven goals conceded yesterday were due to the goalkeeper's errors. Once he regains his proficiency, he should be able to restore his former glory. After 15 minutes, Yoyo was under considerable pressure. Although Zhu Mao Honggui and Lu Shifang defended staunchly, they could not stop the opposing attacks. Liang Guanlian panicked and conceded two more goals. Soon after, Yoyo's Dong Xiaopei made another solo run, scoring a goal. At halftime, the score was 3-2 in favor of the French Businessmen.

A Significant Loss of Energy: Although the final score indicates a clear winner, the overall game was evenly matched. However, due to poor luck, Dong Xiaopei's two attempts were unsuccessful, while the opposing team scored three consecutive goals, making the score 6-2. From then on, Yoyo's morale plummeted, and they struggled to recover. Yoyo's players fought back valiantly, attacking from all sides, making the situation tense. Dong Xiaopei and Shen Baigui each scored a goal, making the score 6-4. In the end, the French Businessmen scored another goal, resulting in a 7-4 victory.

Swap Market Weak

Swap Prices Were Lowered: Because the Gold Exchange held the swap market one day earlier yesterday, it opened for business at 8:00 AM this morning. However, brokers had already started trading before the opening, and the swap prices were still lowered by the shorts, with the gross price estimated to be around 3.5 taels. It then rose to 3.7-8 qian. When trading started at 3.65 taels, longs were willing to swap out, gradually reducing the price, with the final price being 2.2-3 qian. Longs and shorts both had transactions. However, the situation was relatively calm, with no activity in the November contract. The opening price was 733.25 taels, and the closing price was 29.2 qian, a decrease of 3.3 taels compared to the previous day. This was due to the shift to the December contract.

December's Market Was Ordinary: Yesterday, the December contract went on the market, but the situation was mediocre and slightly weak, remaining below 730 taels. From morning to noon, the price difference was only a few qian, and brokerages and speculators did not engage in large transactions. The initial opening was neither good nor bad. Although silver bars fell, forward prices still rose. Foreign cotton and foreign stocks had already surged. Foreign exchange was being extended, and demand in the market was not smooth, while sellers seemed active, frequently lowering prices. However, the Central Bank widely purchased spot goods, totaling about 700 bars, priced at 28 to 28.5 taels. Dadecheng, Tongfeng, Yongtai, and Kangrun sold these to offset forward contracts. However, it was heard that delivery was limited to November and December. The market price was not particularly favorable. Due to the market being closed on Saturday and the complex conditions during the week, the price fluctuated around 30 taels. The overseas silver market had slight fluctuations from time to time, with the lowest price on Tuesday being 727 taels and the highest price on Wednesday being 736 taels. The entire week saw a fluctuation of only 9 taels. Looking back, the result was slightly higher than the previous weekend, by 1.1 qian. The situation for yesterday morning is recorded below:

The Weekend Saw Heavy Fluctuations in Foreign Cents 131

Yesterday was Saturday, and banks were only open for half a day as usual, closing in the afternoon. Although the market traded throughout the day, the afternoon session was naturally quiet due to the banks being closed. However, at this time, the price of foreign cents was unstable, and without bank intervention, there were inevitably irregular price movements. Yesterday morning's fall in cents was due to sluggish buying demand, while the afternoon's rise was due to customers having uses for them but being unable to obtain them from banks.

Last Week's American Cotton 138

Government Estimate Increases and Market Falls

New York, October 14th dispatch, the cotton market conditions for the week are as follows: The government cotton production report estimated an increase in production, and the speculative longs were initially unprepared for this, causing great disturbance. As a result, they sold off one after another, and soon the positions were closed out. However, before the holiday on Wednesday, due to purchases by peers, and because of unfavorable weather in the South, and reports of spot cotton sales in the interior, coupled with the fact that the number of hedges was less than the shorts covering, the price rose slightly. In other respects, buying interest was limited, followed by slightly more hedging. The wheat and securities markets were both weak, the climate was favorable for cotton production, and the theory that severe frost was plaguing the Northwest and North-Central regions of the cotton belt was gradually being dismissed. As a result, cotton prices weakened again. A major cotton grower believes that there has not been much frost in the pest-infested areas, and that it has not had much impact to reduce pests for next season. Domestic fabric industry statistics show that inventories in September decreased by about 23.5%, but the cotton market did not experience any impact as a result. Grain and Rice Market in Shanghai Turns Firm

Yesterday, the rice market in South Shanghai saw about 20 establishments from Xilu source. Transactions on the main street were lively. At one point, Baitaoxin rice and other goods rose by 0.2 yuan. Du Yangjian rice sales were normal, with no change in price. Bai Ge rice was scarce and without market. The total volume for the day was about 2,000 shi.

Yesterday, there were not many goods arriving in Xinzha from inland areas, about 23 or 24 ships. There was some activity on the way to the countryside. Xi Xin rice slightly entered the warehouse, rising by one or two chi. Yixing, Danyang, and Kunshan aged goods had weak interest and prices stabilized. Yang Du Jian did not perform outstandingly and the market presented a downward trend.

Re-export of Foreign Rice Uniquely Popular 140

| Imports of Foreign Rice Not Selling Well |

Yesterday, the price of foreign rice showed no sign of recovery due to the sufficient stock. Saigon short-grain rice continued to weaken by a few cents. However, the number of unreported imports of foreign rice was small because most of them were urged by the customs to report in mid-August. Although there is a lot of stock at the moment, less than half of it is circulating in the market. Among this half, the re-exported goods that have not been reported are less than half. Recently, out-of-town merchants have been inquiring, and even merchants reported that the re-export list has been running low. Yesterday, casual merchants asked about it, and the owner raised prices higher than before, so they were not able to make a deal. However, the fact that re-exported foreign rice uniquely outperformed other rice markets is recognized by the industry. As for the foreign rice that has already been reported, only the main street is active. Yesterday, after it had weakened by two or three cents, it was bought. 800 bags of Saigon No. 1 Zhong Guan rice were sold at 9.023 yuan, and 300 bags of short-grain rice were sold at 7.65 yuan. Hunan rice is not selling well, but a batch is being shipped and will arrive at the market for sale soon.

Flour Market Closing Still Weak 141

Yesterday, the flour market fluctuated in both the upper and lower markets. Short-term prices initially stabilized and then continued to decline, while long-term prices initially remained stable and then rose before falling back to stability. Apart from a difference of about one fen in November and December, the other months only had a few li of fluctuations. Initially, the price of foreign wheat rose. Then, the factories made an agreement to deliver foreign wheat, and the buyers covered their short positions, causing the market to fluctuate. As a result, the short-term market remained weak because of the current low demand and continuous hedging by factories. The price fell by 0.25 fen for the current month, 0.1 fen for next month, 0.05 fen for December, and 0.25 fen for January. For the long-term market, factories did not issue many chips, and customers and short-sellers were buying and covering, so the market did not follow the downward trend of the short-term market. The closing price for February was unchanged, and the price for March rose by 0.025 fen.

Wheat Market Mixed 142

Yesterday, the wheat market was firm in the morning and slightly fluctuated in the afternoon. Recently, the spot market has been weak, and market prices and sentiment are upward. However, after the long-term market weakened slightly, the market was slightly dragged down. The long-term market was strongly shorted by traders due to the arrival of foreign wheat. As a result, the price of the months of October and November was unchanged, December increased by 0.1 fen, and January to March each decreased by 0.02 fen. The current factory sale is still active, with 1,500 bags being issued and purchased by Huafeng Shenda. 3.37 to 3.35 liang was offered for Shaoxing wheat, 3.27 liang for Ying wheat, and 3.4 liang for Suqian wheat.

Sugar Market: More Than 1,000 Bags of Wan Qing Offered

Yesterday, the sugar market was characterized by a general weakness as the exchange rate of Dutch currency was declining. The association's price indication tended towards stability with common grade 24-numbered sugar quoted at 14.875 taels but no deal was made. Higher grade was quoted at 14.975 taels. Fine sugar was at 15 taels. The average number of 18-numbered medium sugar was small, while the price of scarce 20-numbered medium sugar was quoted at 14 taels, but there were not much sales. Northbound Goods, Jinshan Branch Soil Price and Number of Pieces All Rise

Jinshan branches have recently seen a sudden shift towards firmness in the market due to brisk sales. The most rapid increase has been in the price of the flat branch number of pieces. The northern market has released over a thousand cases in recent days, with high-quality goods rising to 28 taels and common goods to 24-25 taels. The price of Yuan branches has also risen, with high-quality goods at 24 taels, medium grade at 21-22 taels, and common grade around 20 taels. As a result, land prices have also been affected. The price of flat branches has increased by 40 yuan, with 28 taels being charged. The price of Yuan branches has increased to 35 yuan, with 25 taels being charged. Therefore, the trend seems to be tightening again. However, the goods from Zhangzhou have not been improved, and the sizes of the pieces vary, which does not suit customer taste. Therefore, the sales in various places are almost entirely occupied by Jinshan branches, which is a pity.

Metal and White Iron Sheet Prices are High and Transactions are Scarce

Yesterday, metal transactions were as flat as before. Northern merchants seemed to be less enthusiastic about purchasing. Factory users and shop business were still bustling, but mostly for small-volume sales. Therefore, the surface situation appeared to be busy. And each city moved, yesterday, more slightly, but recorded its main market conditions below for reference.

White Iron Sheets are Currently Being Sought After. After the price of white iron sheets increased, transactions progressed for a while. However, recently, users have felt that the price is too high and have been hesitant to adopt them. The out-of-town merchants are also cautious because the price of this product is expensive and it is difficult to sell at once. Therefore, in addition to inquiries, they do not dare to purchase, so the future of transactions is very quiet. However, the market price has been able to maintain and has not fallen. British 7-foot sheets are sold at 9.6 fen, 6-foot sheets at 8.2 fen, American 48 sheets at 15.5 taels, thick-patterned 28-gauge British sheets at 11.75 taels, American sheets at 16 taels, 26-gauge British sheets at 11.5 taels, American sheets at 15 taels, and 24-gauge British sheets at 11.5 taels, American sheets at 14 taels.

Round Nails are Still Selling Poorly. The sales of round nails have been very sluggish recently. Although the nominal price has not fluctuated much, the substance is very weak. The biggest reason is actually the impact of the brisk sales of locally made nails. It is reported that only about 200 buckets have been sold in recent weeks.
