Chen Ronggong Views the Sichuan Situation 147

The Reasons are Complex and the Solution is Difficult

What is the Sin of the Sichuan People to Suffer This Calamity?

Since the conflict between Liu Xiang and Liu Wenhui in Sichuan occurred, the inside story has been heard from afar, and opinions vary. The reporter of the New Voice News Agency, in order to make readers understand the situation in Sichuan, visited Chen Ronggong, a revolutionary elder from Sichuan and former commander of the Fourth Division, yesterday afternoon. Chen has the grace of being a teacher and friend to Deng Tian and others, and many of the middle-ranking officers in Sichuan were his students. Therefore, although he has retired to Shanghai and is absorbed in calligraphy and painting, he still receives news from Sichuan from time to time and is very knowledgeable. The following is a summary of what he said:

The History of the Two Lius. Liu Wenhui and Liu Xiang were originally uncle and nephew. Before the establishment of the Nanjing government, Liu Xiang was originally the commander of the Second Division of the Sichuan Army, while Liu Wenhui was only a brigade commander. The uncle and nephew have always established their own banners and followed different paths, but they still protected each other from time to time. Therefore, internally, they schemed against each other to expand their power, and externally, they adopted different tactics to shift attention and protect their positions. For example, Liu Wenhui's previous support for Yan Feng was later secured by Liu Xiang's power, and conversely, Liu Wenhui would also come out to protect Liu Xiang. Therefore, the general public in Sichuan regarded the interaction between the two Lius as a double act on stage, and they always called it "playing a double act." In fact, both Lius were taking advantage of the opportunity to increase their power. Therefore, every time a Sichuan war broke out, it was always at a time when the country was in turmoil, so that the central government and other parties would have no time to pay attention to it.

The Real Cause of This Conflict. Judging from the past history of the two Lius, it seems that there would be no possibility of conflict when neither party had the strength to unify Sichuan. The reasons for this sudden move are more than one. On the one hand, Liu Wenhui recently purchased arms and ammunition from abroad, which were detained by Liu Xiang when they reached Sichuan. Liu Wenhui went to Chongqing and sat there for a day to demand them, but Liu Xiang repeatedly excused himself, claiming that it was done by his subordinates. As a result, although he promised to investigate and return them, he only made empty promises and never fulfilled them. Therefore, Liu Wenhui left in anger and prepared to use force to deal with it. When Liu Xiang heard about this, he was unwilling to show weakness. However, at that time, they were only showing off their strength to each other. Later, because various parties saw that there was a gap between them, they also provoked them, and it turned into a real split. Therefore, the conflict between the two Lius can be said to have been made real by pretending. On the other hand, Liu Xiang has shown considerable goodwill towards the central government in recent years, such as sending his division commander Wang Luquan's troops to western Hubei to suppress bandits. Therefore, he wants to take the opportunity to use the power of the central government to unify Sichuan.

Comparison of the Strength of the Two Sides. Judging from the strength of the two sides, Liu Xiang has five divisions plus a mixed brigade, with a total of about 130,000 people. The arms and ammunition are sufficient, but the weapons are slightly old. In addition, there are four small warships, which also have artillery positions, and are used for patrol. There are also thirteen aircraft, including two bombers, three reconnaissance aircraft, and the rest are civil aviation aircraft, which are also convenient for transporting essential items. The number of tank cars is also quite a few. Furthermore, Liu Xiang's subordinates have one characteristic, that is, Liu Mou's brigade is known as the "Divine Soldiers." Like the military advisors of each army, whenever there is a military operation, the decision is first made by the commander of this brigade. As to how effective it is, outsiders see it as truly mysterious, but Liu Xiang absolutely trusts it. Once, when Liu Xiang was conducting an exercise and dropping bombs, he asked this brigade commander about the outcome in advance. He was firmly told that it was unfavorable and advised Liu to change the date. Therefore, although Liu still went to supervise, he followed the advice of those around him and stayed away. As a result, on that day, the aircraft dropped bombs, and because the direction was inaccurate, more than 90 soldiers were killed and injured when the bombs exploded. If Liu had not avoided in advance, he would have been involved. Since then, Liu Xiang has relied on him more and more. Therefore, the people of Sichuan call him the "God of the Army, Navy, and Air Force." As for the discipline and training of Liu Xiang's troops, they are far inferior to Liu Wenhui's efforts. Liu Wenhui has two divisions plus a mixed brigade. The organization and training are the same as Yuan Shikai's Machang training system. However, the division commander does not have the power to command directly. Each division has two brigades, and one brigade must be its confidant command. The number of people is equal to Liu Xiang, and the equipment is the latest model, but there are no aircraft, warships, or tank cars. However, in terms of the strength of the armed forces themselves, Liu Wenhui's strength seems to be stronger than Liu Xiang's. Furthermore, in terms of economy, Liu Wenhui's defense area, because it is in the Chengdu area, is extremely abundant. Liu Xiang is far inferior to him. Recently, it has been learned that because of the failure of the previous shipment of equipment, Liu Wenhui has already opened up another route and is taking another route through Yunnan, Guizhou, and Guiyang.

The Attitude of Various Armies in Sichuan. Since the two Lius have started a conflict, the rest of the armies, depending on the distance, actually have the power to influence the overall situation. The leaders of these armies who are most noteworthy are Deng Xihou, Tian Songyao, Liu Cunhou, Yang Sen, Luo Zezhou, and Li Qixiang. Deng Xihou and Tian Songyao, because they and Liu Wenhui graduated from the Baoding Military Academy, often join together because of the same academic system, forming a group with deep ties, a defensive alliance. Therefore, what has been reported in the newspapers recently that Deng and Tian are helping Liu Xiang to defeat Liu Wenhui has another inside story. Because Liu, Tian, and Deng's troops are all near Chengdu, things must be approved by all three before they can be implemented. If Deng and Tian help Liu Xiang to suppress Liu Wenhui, in the interests of these two themselves, they must not do this. Therefore, the reason why they have not abruptly changed their usual state is simply to send secret messages to the two Lius, engaging in provocation, hoping to create opportunities for themselves. Because Liu Wenhui's defense area is richer than anyone else's, the position towards Liu Xiang is more obvious. If this split turns into a real war, they will take the opportunity to occupy it. From a direct perspective, they will not be used by the two Lius. As for Liu Cunhou and Yang Sen, judging from their history and attitude, they seem to tend towards Liu Xiang, but it seems that the time is still too early. Luo Zezhou and Li Qixiang were originally the old troops of Deng Xihou, and they have not completely broken away from the relationship until now. Therefore, although they are now on Liu Xiang's side, they will certainly only follow Deng's lead in the future.

War Has No Good Outcome. From the above, it can be seen that the two sides are evenly matched, and their strength can be said to be evenly matched. Moreover, in terms of terrain, Liu Xiang's center of gravity is in Chongqing, located in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River, and transportation must be more difficult. Liu Wenhui's troops are all in the upper reaches, with a commanding position. Therefore, Chengdu is suitable for attacking, and Chongqing has natural defensive works because it is surrounded by rivers on three sides, so it is suitable for defending. However, judging from the current situation, Liu Xiang is seeking a quick victory because of his more complete military equipment, and Liu Wenhui is still purchasing aircraft, etc. Although the contact and initiation seem to have been initiated by him, it is not actually the case. He is still waiting for a month before he can implement the attack, because Wang Lingji's troops who were suppressing bandits in western Hubei have recently been hastily concentrated in the Yichang area. It can be seen that Liu Xiang is preparing for war. However, the result will inevitably be like this, rising and falling, only suffering the Sichuan people.

It is Not Easy to Resolve the Sichuan Situation. It is currently heard that the central government is preparing to send senior officials to Sichuan to mediate. Judging from the above-mentioned complex reasons, it is feared that there will be no solution even if they go. The two Lius want to take advantage of the national difficulties such as suppressing bandits and the unrest in the Lu war to engage in expanding their own power, and there is a reason for what they do. It is by no means something that can be resolved with a few words. Therefore, to resolve the Sichuan situation, we must wait for the whole country to be peaceful, try our best to organize a strong Sichuan provincial government, return the political and economic power of the defense areas of each army to the provincial government, and then send troops to the border between Tibet and Kang, so that there can be a considerable solution. As for the people of Sichuan, because they have been exploited to the extreme for many years by the two Lius, such as various taxes, some of which have been in place for more than sixty years, it can be understood. Therefore, the Sichuan fellow villagers in Shanghai, in view of the fact that their hometown men have been in dire straits for 21 years, all hope that there will be a fundamental reform in the Sichuan situation.

On the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway

Hu Hongji Dies 148

Hu Hongji, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, along with his friend Zhang Zongkang and a certain Westerner, etc., in two private cars, left Shanghai for Hangzhou yesterday afternoon. They were driving along the Shanghai-Hangzhou highway and arrived at Haiyan Station at about 5 o'clock. Zhang Zongkang and another person were in the front car, driven by a Westerner, and they were driving very fast. Hu and Zhang Shoupei and two others followed behind, driven by Hu. Because it was getting late and they were anxious to get to Hangzhou, the car overtook Haiyan Station by three miles. At that time, the road was narrow, the road was rugged, and it was not easy to pass. Hu's car overturned to the left and jumped out of a stone embankment three zhang high, crashing into the beach. The area was very desolate. Fortunately, a stack material car from the Hangzhou-Pinghu road was passing by and heard cries for help, so they stopped and rescued them. Hu and Zhang were seriously injured, and the other two were slightly injured. They were accompanied to the Haiyan Hospital by the stationmaster of Haiyan Station. Hu died due to ineffective treatment, and Zhang's life is also in danger. Hu's body was parked in the car slot of Haiyan Station. However, Zhang Zongkang and others in the front car were unaware of what had happened behind them. After arriving in Hangzhou, they received a telegram from the stationmaster of Haiyan Station, and immediately went to rescue them with Dr. Sutler of Guangji Hospital. They returned to Hangzhou after two hours. Zhang Zongkang urgently reported the situation to Hu's house by long-distance telephone.

Huang Shaoxiong and Gan Naikang's Conversation 149

Huang: Diplomatic Victory Still Requires Our Own Efforts

Gan: Internal Affairs Conference to Be Held on December 12th

According to the Guowen News Agency, Minister of Internal Affairs and concurrently Minister of Communications Huang Shaoxiong and Vice Minister Gan Naikang arrived in Shanghai together yesterday morning from Nanjing to discuss departmental affairs. Yesterday, reporters visited them separately. Huang and Gan are scheduled to return to Nanjing tomorrow (Monday). The following is a record of their conversations:

Huang Shaoxiong spoke to reporters at the Cangzhou Hotel on Jing'an Temple Road. When asked about the situation in the central government regarding internal affairs and communications, he stated, "I am here to discuss departmental affairs. I arrived in Shanghai this morning. It is not necessarily just about internal affairs. Matters concerning the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, the International Radio Station, and the Postal Service, all of which fall under the Ministry of Communications in Shanghai, are all being discussed." He also mentioned that Mr. Zhen Ru had requested to retire from his position as Minister of Communications, and the central government had asked him to take on the role concurrently. However, due to the heavy workload, he felt unable to handle both positions and had repeatedly requested the central government to appoint a replacement. As a result, he has not been relieved of the concurrent position and is still serving in both roles. He did not visit Mr. Wang (Jingwei) because the hospital was refusing visitors. As for whether he will go abroad and whether the Political Council will make changes due to personnel issues, he had not heard anything and was not clear on the details. In summary, both the internal affairs and communications departments are currently being reorganized. Li Zongren previously sent representatives Wen Qiaosheng and Yang Zhuang to Nanjing and Wuhan to meet with various parties to discuss border defense and the military situation in Guangxi. However, this happened a month ago, and the representatives have already returned to Guangxi. The central government has ordered American wheat, and there is a special department within the government to handle food matters. However, the total wheat production in China is only between 100 and 200 million tons, which is insufficient to be supplemented by foreign grain. This year, there has been a slight bumper harvest on both sides of the Yangtze River, so some people believe that the import of American wheat will affect domestic agricultural production and have risen up in opposition. In reality, if the purchased American wheat is averaged out and combined with domestic production, it is still not enough to meet the needs of the entire country. The American wheat will naturally be distributed to provinces with a shortage of food. Due to tariff and transportation issues, it cannot reach food-deficient areas in one step. Areas with good harvests, seeing this large batch of American wheat passing through, believe that its sale will suppress domestic agricultural production and therefore oppose it. I have no comments on the report. It is currently being studied and considered by the central government. However, I personally have one thing to say: the report can be studied, or it cannot be studied. Everything depends on our own efforts. If we can find ways to reorganize the existing military and political affairs, it will be enough to overcome the difficulties." After speaking, he shook hands and bid farewell. Lin Shi, Yang Jianping, and others also visited. Huang is scheduled to return to Nanjing tomorrow (the 17th).

Gan Naikang spoke about the Ministry of Internal Affairs. Yesterday, when reporters visited Gan Naikang at his residence in Shanghai, they asked about the recent situation of the Ministry of Internal Affairs. According to Gan, the Ministry of Internal Affairs will convene a national internal affairs conference. At that time, civil affairs directors from various provinces, directors of public security, land, and health bureaus from various cities, as well as experts, will gather together. The Ministry of Internal Affairs has now dispatched personnel in three groups for inspection. The first group is the North China group, consisting of Gan himself, Section Chiefs Liang and Luo, and a technician. They will depart soon, first going to Zouping in Shandong, then to Tianjin and Dingxian, and then return to Nanjing via Kaifeng. The second group is the Jiangsu-Zhejiang group, consisting of three people including a department director, who will inspect along the Shanghai-Nanjing-Hangzhou railway and then to Nantong. The third group is the Hunan-Hubei-Henan-Anhui group, consisting of four people including Section Chief Zheng, who will be responsible for investigating the rehabilitation issues in the bandit areas. The inspection will be completed within one month. After returning to Nanjing, the Ministry of Internal Affairs will begin drafting proposals. Four proposals have already been drafted: (1) Implement a conscription system for the militia and security forces, similar to what is currently being done in Guangxi, to deal with national crises and strengthen national defense in the future. (2) Local self-government, including organizational and industrial development. (3) Rehabilitation of bandit areas, such as land consolidation. (4) Strict reorganization of local political systems. The conference secretariat has now been established. The conference organization will be passed by the Executive Yuan at its meeting next Tuesday. The conference is scheduled to be held on December 10th in the capital. This internal affairs conference will be different from the past. We will implement the resolutions with all our energy. I will return to Nanjing tomorrow (the 17th)." After speaking, he bade farewell.

Important Statements by Representatives Ma and Li 151

Ma et al. are military and political leaders appointed by the state.

Their names were not listed in the public announcement of the People's National Salvation Army.

Yesterday, the newspaper reported that the public announcement of the Northeastern People's National Salvation Army listed the names of Generals Ma Zhanshan and Li Du at the end. Yesterday, the reporter from the Nisshin News Agency specially visited Ma Zhanshan's representative Tian Xiuqiao and Li Du's representative Liu Piguang at their residence to inquire about the truth. According to them, on the 14th of this month (the day before yesterday), the newspapers in this city published a public announcement from the Northeastern People's National Salvation Army led by Cheng Yun, Deng Jianzhong, and Shen Zhifu, requesting assistance, listing Mr. Ma and Mr. Li as committee members. Upon investigation, Chairman Ma and Commanders Li and Ding are all officially appointed military and political leaders of Jilin and Heilongjiang by the state, in charge of the military and political affairs of Jilin and Heilongjiang. They have never joined any organization, nor have they ever been listed in any public announcement or declaration. Moreover, Mr. Ma and Mr. Li have already issued a public announcement to the outside world and sent it to us (Tian and Liu) to be responsible for its publication. The fact that the Northeastern People's National Salvation Army listed their names in the telegram this time was neither telegraphed by Mr. Ma and Mr. Li, nor did we know anything about it beforehand. Mr. Ma and Mr. Li will not be responsible for any of their actions. I hope that all sectors will not misunderstand."

Yesterday 153

Four Organizations Welcomed Mrs. Muir

and Brigade Commander Weng Zhaoyuan and Chen Wulie

Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the Shanghai All-Circles National Salvation United Association, the Republic of China National Salvation Organizations United Association, the Northeastern Volunteer Army Relief Association, and the China Aviation Construction Association, held a reception at Tan Haiqiu's residence at No. 15 Jissi Fei'er Road to welcome Mrs. Muir, Brigade Commander Weng Zhaoyuan, and Mr. Chen Wulie. Tan's residence is a Western-style building, but its exterior is completely in the ancient Chinese style, combining magnificence with solemnity. There are rockeries and fountains in front of the house, making it a quiet and elegant place, which is the most suitable place for receiving distinguished guests. After 3:00 PM, guests arrived one after another and were greeted by Dr. Yin Zhiling. The host entertained the guests with wireless radio music. At that time, the heavens were unkind and it suddenly rained heavily, which greatly disappointed everyone. Fortunately, the rain stopped and the sun came out, and the weather became more harmonious. Mrs. Muir arrived at 3:30 PM and shook hands with the welcomers one by one. She then went into the reception room to sit and chat for a while. Mrs. Muir is about 50 years old and wears simple and unpretentious clothes. The reception table was arranged in a T-shape, with flowers placed beside it. Over a hundred people attended, including Mrs. Muir, Weng Zhaoyuan, Chen Wulie, Yin Zhiling, Wen Zongyao, Xu Jigong, Yin Zhufu, Sun Bolan, Tan Bozhi, Tan Haiqiu, Tan Zhiyong, Chen Dingyuan, Huang Hongjun, Hu Zushun, Lin Jiyong, He Yongyuan, Zhang Pei, and others. Female guests accounted for one-fifth of the attendees. When Mrs. Muir took her seat, reporters from various newspapers competed to take pictures. Mrs. Muir stood among the female guests, as if trying to avoid being photographed by the reporters. After taking their seats, Li Cishan presided over the meeting, Ling Xianchang translated, and Xu Tongye recorded. The chairman reported the purpose of the welcome, mainly stating that Mrs. Muir, because the 19th Route Army stood on the side of justice and fought for the survival of the Chinese nation in the Battle of Shanghai, Mrs. Muir, representing the German women's community, traveled thousands of miles to China to express her sympathy. Not only is the 19th Route Army grateful for Mrs. Muir's kindness, but the people of the whole country are also grateful. Brigade Commander Weng is admired by countries all over the world and has now handed over his position as brigade commander. He will soon go to Europe and the United States to study. Brigade Commander Weng made contributions in the Battle of Shanghai, and there were no defensive structures in Wusong. The entire brigade had only a few thousand soldiers, and only eight hundred soldiers on the front line were able to hold out for more than thirty days. His reputation has spread far and wide throughout the world. In the future, Brigade Commander Weng's work can give us even more sympathy. Mr. Chen Wulie is an old friend of Dr. Sun Yat-sen and once used huge sums of money to support the revolution. He spared no effort in promoting Chinese culture in Siam. Our compatriots who live overseas owe much to Mr. Chen. Mr. Chen felt the greatness of the anti-Japanese work and donated a great deal to the Northeastern Volunteer Army. We hope that when Mr. Chen returns to Siam, he will be able to convey the good intentions of his compatriots in the motherland to the overseas Chinese." Mrs. Muir answered in English, saying, "Ladies and gentlemen, I am very happy to have this opportunity to speak with you today. However, there is one thing I must correct to you: I do not represent the German people, but the people of all cultured countries in the world. People in Europe did not know anything about the situation in China until after the anti-Japanese war. Now, people all over Europe admire the bravery of the Chinese people and admire their ability to fight for justice and humanity. Anyone in the world can see that. Chinese people, Chinese consuls, and vice consuls all interact with us. Although most of the Chinese in Europe are laborers, they are very sincere, frugal, brave, and kind. Therefore, we value them. Since I came from Germany, I have passed through Italy, Spain, Luzon, Guangzhou, and other places. Especially in Luzon, I saw that the major banks were all in the hands of the Chinese, and there were many laborers who were honest and not deceitful. These people are the easiest to admire because they are all truly capable of saving China. Today, I cannot talk about Chinese culture because China has more than 4,000 years of culture. How was Germany 4,000 years ago? No one can imagine it. And China has more than 4,000 years of culture and 4,000 years of history. How can we allow the Japanese to lose the three northeastern provinces? As for General Weng Zhaoyuan, I have met him once. Although we did not talk much, I knew at a glance that General Weng was a calm and brave man. When he defended Wusong, we admired him very much. In the literature of all countries in the world, there are works about Weng. This time, General Weng's trip abroad to study aviation is also a necessary plan for China. Because the future war of the world will focus on air combat, China must first strengthen its aviation, and General Weng is the most suitable person to engage in aviation. Today, Mr. Chen Wulie, who is also welcomed here, I have not met, but when I was in Luzon, I heard his name. Major banks and merchants all expressed their respect for Mr. Chen. I deeply know that Chinese people pay great attention to justice. Because we are in Europe, far away from the ocean, we do not know who is right and who is wrong in this Sino-Japanese war, so it is difficult to speak out. Therefore, I hope that China will engage in foreign publicity to clarify the truth." Finally, Wang Qingxun played a harmonica piece for the soldiers of the 19th Route Army, followed by representatives Weng Zhaoyuan and Chen Wulie, who delivered replies before the meeting adjourned.

Farewell Banquet for Luo Jingyou by the Security Corps 156

Yesterday afternoon at 5:00 PM, the management committee of the city's security corps and the corps leaders and deputy leaders held a farewell banquet for the former chairman of the committee, Mr. Luo Jingyou, at Yizhixiang. During the banquet, Standing Committee Member Yao Mulian delivered a speech on behalf of all the security corps members, stating that since its inception a year ago, the corps' affairs have been managed by Chairman Luo with great effort. In this difficult time for the city, he has not only been able to fulfill his duties and protect local safety and tranquility, but also made significant developments in the organization and economy of the corps. Today, Chairman Luo is being promoted, and the corps members are overcome with the sadness of parting. On behalf of the wood corps members, I wish Chairman Luo a bright future." After the speech, Mr. Luo stood up and replied, "Comrades, Jingyou has worked with you for a long time, and now that I am about to say goodbye, I cannot help but feel a deep sense of reluctance. You comrades are all keenly aware of the meaning and mission of the security corps, the local connections, and the expectations of the public, and you have been working diligently to fulfill them. There is no need for me to say more. However, I would like to mention that the Shanghai Security Corps was reorganized from the early commercial corps and established during the Qi-Lu War. After being reorganized and developed by former Mayor Zhang, the regulations were clearly defined. Over the years, it has been able to show considerable achievements in assisting the military and police, maintaining local order, and protecting the people, which is obvious to everyone. Public opinion is satisfied, and there is a sense of trust. This is all due to the joint efforts and hard work of the past officials and comrades, who have fulfilled their responsibilities. It is not accidental. This year, with the outbreak of the January 28th Incident, the military and police worked hard to resist the invaders, and the situation was very serious. The mission of the Security Corps was also unusually tense. Maintaining local safety and tranquility and maintaining social order, all that should be done was done to the best of our ability, to supplement the shortcomings of the military and police, so as to complete the work of assisting and consolidating defense. Therefore, the corps in the war zone inevitably suffered heavy losses, and even those in the non-war zone were gradually stagnating due to the tight funding. Fortunately, Committee Member Yao Mulian, Committee Member Wang Binyan, and other committee members worked hard to support it, and Mayor Wu provided practical guidance and supervision to promote progress, so that it did not fall. Jingyou has repeatedly been entrusted by former Mayor Zhang and Mayor Wu to prepare for reorganization. I am ashamed of my meager abilities and have not been able to help. I am grateful to all comrades for not abandoning me and for pushing me to be a standing committee member during this difficult time. Jingyou declined but was forced to accept the difficult task. Since taking office, I have worked hard day and night, following Mayor Wu's instructions and discussing with all comrades to believe that the local merchants and people have suffered this catastrophe and have no time to rest. The only thing to do is to first reorganize the various teams in the non-war zone, and then resume the establishment of the teams in the war zone, and unify the corps, guide training, to lay the foundation and plan for progress. We have also formulated a revival plan based on the corps' losses, and submitted it to the municipal government for transfer to the Shanghai Post-War Committee to allocate funds to purchase equipment and military supplies, so as to supplement and strengthen our strength. The people's self-defense must cultivate the people's martial power, and Shanghai should not be regarded as a slow plan under the current situation. Today, the inspection of the district teams in the city has been completed, and the war zone losses and revival plans have been successively approved by the municipal government. Although the post-war financial reduction has not yet been fully realized, following this policy, gradual progress will surely live up to the expectations of Mayor Wu and all comrades. Jingyou is not talented, and I originally wanted to follow all comrades to complete the work. However, due to the urgent call to Wuhan, I had to leave in a hurry. There are things I want to say that cannot be fully expressed in writing. I am even more grateful to the leaders of the corps for bestowing me with a farewell banquet and presenting me with a silver tripod. How grateful I am! Now, I am fortunate that Mr. Zhang Tingjun is in charge of Jingyou's affairs, and his achievements should be a hundred times greater than in the past. It is foreseeable that although Jingyou is leaving, the corps' affairs will continue to progress. I only hope that all comrades will seize the opportunity to work hard and jointly achieve great things. Jingyou is looking forward to it. I would like to attach the meaning of the farewell speech of the ancients to express my foolishness. I hope you will understand."

Jidong Postal Items are Delivered as Usual 159

China and Russia agree to ship by sea via Vladivostok

Packets sealed by the Suifenhe and Shanghai bureaus

After the postal blockade was implemented in the Northeast, except for Daheihe and other places along the Heilongjiang River, which belong to the defense area of the National Army Ma Zhanshan, and within the South Manchuria Railway Zone, where postal services can be carried out as usual, postal services in the other two provinces of Liaoning and Jilin have been suspended. According to news from the postal headquarters in this city, Suifenhe, Dongning, Muling Station, Xiachengzi, Muling, Pingyang Town, Mishan, Boli, Raohe, Tongjiang, Xiaosuifen, Xinglong Town, Maqiaohe, Lishu Town, Banjiehezi, Hulin, Baoqing, Fuyuan, and other places in eastern Jilin are still under the jurisdiction of officials appointed by our central government. Although postal parcels and remittances in these places have been suspended, ordinary postal services, such as the delivery of letters, cannot be interrupted. The Ministry of Communications of our country and the Soviet Russian postal authorities in Moscow have agreed on a method for delivering postal items, deciding that the postal bureaus in Suifenhe and Shanghai will collect and seal packets and forward them separately to various places, and transport them by ship via Vladivostok. All registered and ordinary letters can be sent as usual, and postage will be charged according to domestic rates. Yesterday, the general headquarters had instructed postal bureaus in various places to comply.

Construction 162

Actively Proceeding in the Central Area of the City

Establishment of a Construction Fund Management Committee

The construction project in the central area of the city was halted due to the January 28th Incident. After the signing of the ceasefire agreement, the Municipal Bureau of Public Works immediately resumed work according to the original plan. The construction of the new municipal government building resumed on July 1st, and the road earthwork project within the first batch of land requisition resumed on September 1st. The Municipal Government, in accordance with the principle of transparency in finances and to promote the construction of the area, established the Central Area Construction Fund Management Committee, appointing Cai Zengji, Director of the Finance Bureau, and Shen Yi, Chairman of the Central Area Construction Committee, and inviting Mr. Lin Kanghou, as well as electing Dong Chengdao and Xia Pingfang as representatives of the landowners, to serve as members of the committee, responsible for managing the construction funds of the area, demonstrating the determination to build a new urban area. The committee has also resolved to expedite the collection of land prices to meet the payment of construction costs. The project plans and progress of the area, as obtained from various sources, are detailed below: Project Plans: The construction project within the first batch of land requisition in the central area of the city is divided into roads, ditches, bridges, landscaping, and buildings, and will be carried out in three phases. The first phase involves filling the entire subgrade and 40% of the six-meter-wide asphalt road surface, 50% of the ditches, and building bridges and planting trees. The entire subgrade is expected to be completed by the end of November this year, and the road surface and ditches will be completed by September next year.

Progress: Since the resumption of work, the Municipal Bureau of Public Works has been actively supervising the progress of the project. The completed projects include the buildings of the Central Area Construction Management Office. The projects currently underway include the new municipal government building, the police station building of the Public Security Bureau, and the subgrade and roadbed projects. Other projects such as bridge construction and ditching are also being planned, and several thousand saplings have been ordered from the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum in Nanjing for the layout of parks, which will arrive in Shanghai soon. However, most of the ongoing projects are currently focused on the subgrade, so they are not easily noticeable. Once the road surface, bridge, and ditch projects are implemented, there will be a new look.

Pickled Meat Industry Opposes the Collection of Pickled Pork Inspection Fees

Answers from Directors Cai and Hu 163

Finance Bureau Director Cai Zengji and Health Bureau Director Hu Hongji sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, stating: "Greetings, we have received your letter No. 149, which states that on September 30th, the Municipal Pickled Meat Industry Association stated in a letter that the Finance and Health Bureaus have recently suddenly levied pickled pork inspection fees, disregarding the difficulties of merchants. All pickled meat merchants in the city are greatly angered and unanimously oppose it, believing that at a time when internal and external troubles are pressing and the social economy is precarious, all industries are declining, and doing business is already difficult. Now, the authorities want to use inspection as a pretext to extort money, adding unnecessary burdens. The pickled meat merchants know that they are unable to bear the burden and will be forced to close down. The authorities will only alienate the people and create disputes, which is not a blessing for society or the country. Therefore, our association previously sent a letter to your chamber, asking you to understand the difficulties of merchants and urge the municipal authorities to realize their error and withdraw the proposal to collect pickled pork inspection fees. Now, the municipal authorities insist on their decision, disregarding the difficulties of merchants, not only refusing to cancel the fees but also actively collecting them, destroying business operations and disrupting the market. Those who should protect the people are harming them, and those who should benefit the country are harming it. All pickled meat merchants in the city have gathered at our association and unanimously resolved to oppose it. If the authorities disregard public opinion and act arbitrarily, they will not hesitate to make any sacrifices. We have always admired your chamber as a guarantor of the business community and believe that you will understand the difficulties of merchants and provide protection. Therefore, we reiterate the reasons in detail as follows: (1) Shandong is the main source of pickled pork, and the slaughter tax and inspection are strict there. As raw fresh pork, it has already undergone strict inspection, and inferior goods have long been eliminated. Only the best quality pork is salted and pickled to produce pickled pork for export. Therefore, in fact, pickled pork is generally of good quality and has already been inspected, so there is no need for further inspection. Moreover, the fees are exorbitant, and merchants cannot afford to bear them, so they will inevitably continue to raise prices. Foreign goods, such as salmon, are taxed very simply and cheaply. Therefore, this repeated inspection is tantamount to a disguised method of blocking domestic products and encouraging foreign goods. The hygiene is not actually improved, and the fees are collected under false pretenses. This is the first reason for opposing the inspection. (2) People only worry about the safety of fresh meat, but pickled meat has never been a source of danger. In Shanghai, pickled pork has been sold for hundreds of years, and many people eat it, but no one has ever been harmed by eating pickled pork. Pickled pork is pickled in salt in a vat and cannot produce microorganisms, so it is definitely safe and there is no doubt about it. Now, the authorities are concerned about the health of the people, but there are many things in society that harm public health, and they do not actively clean them up. Instead, they want to impose repeated inspections and fees on pickled pork, which is safe in both fact and custom, to burden our people and our merchants. How can this be? Furthermore, people who have a reduced appetite after illness often use pickled meat to stimulate their appetite because it tastes good and can increase their appetite. It is similar in effect and taste to Western butter and dried game, which further proves that pickled pork is a safe food and does not harm health. This is the second reason for opposing the inspection. (3) Pickled pork in Shanghai comes from other ports, and the pickled meat merchants in this city only sell on behalf of the guest merchants, earning a small commission. The guest merchants incur large costs in transporting pickled pork, and in recent years, the price of rice, firewood, and other goods has been high, so their expenses are large and their profits are small. Moreover, they travel across the ocean to Shanghai, where they are often threatened by pirates. The risks are many. It is already seen as a difficult journey. At a time when the situation is unstable, business operations are even more difficult. Therefore, the supply of pickled pork to this city has already decreased, and businesses are declining. If the authorities want to create inspection fees, it will be even more difficult to do business. The guest merchants have already stopped shipping goods upon hearing about the proposal to collect inspection fees. If the inspection fees are implemented, pickled pork will inevitably disappear from Shanghai. The authorities are no different from cutting off the people's food supply. Anyone with a heart would not do this. This is the third reason for opposing the inspection. (4) Since the September 18th Incident, business has declined sharply, especially for pickled meat merchants. This is because pickled meat is not a daily necessity, and the people's economic difficulties have affected it. The wounds of the January 28th Incident have further deepened the suffering of the people in Shanghai, leading to more business failures. All debts in the war zone have not been recovered, and it is difficult to recover debts even outside the war zone. The merchants are barely maintaining their businesses for the sake of the livelihoods of thousands of employees. If new taxes are levied and inspection fees are added, the merchants will not be able to bear the burden and will have to close down and seek other livelihoods. This is the fourth reason for opposing the inspection. The above reasons are all based on facts. All pickled meat merchants in the city are determined to oppose it to the end. The situation is urgent. We ask your chamber to understand the difficulties of merchants and quickly request the municipal authorities to immediately cancel the decision to collect inspection fees in order to maintain business operations and alleviate the difficulties of merchants." According to this, the two industries of pickled meat and ham have repeatedly expressed opposition since your bureau proposed the plan. Because they did not list the reasons, they were not conveyed. Now, according to what they have stated, they believe that pickled pork is transported from other ports after being pickled, and is wrapped in salt. Although it looks rough, it is definitely not rotten. It has been sold in Shanghai for a long time, and those who eat it have not had any adverse impressions. Therefore, there is no need for inspection. After the January 28th Incident, the city's business has been in a slump, and the pickled pork industry is no exception. At a time when both supply and sales are weak, it will be even more difficult to maintain business operations if inspection fees are added. Therefore, there should be no inspection. Considering the situation, there are some reasonable grounds. It is appropriate to inform your bureau of the situation and request that you consider it and submit it so that the implementation can be temporarily delayed to alleviate the difficulties of merchants. I am deeply grateful. In addition to sending separate letters, etc., it is hereby approved. After investigation, the main purpose of the Pickled Meat Industry Association in requesting the cessation of inspection of meat products entering the city is not that meat products entering the city should not be inspected, but to hope that the collection of pickled pork inspection fees can be reduced. It can be seen that the association does not know that the city's inspection of meat products entering the city is to improve public health and is an inherent function of health administration. However, there are many misunderstandings about the meaning of this case, so a detailed explanation should be given to clarify the truth and dispel doubts. The answers are as follows: 1. The original letter states that the Finance and Health Bureaus have recently suddenly levied pickled pork inspection fees, disregarding the difficulties of merchants. All pickled meat merchants in the city are greatly angered and unanimously oppose it, etc. The inspection of meat products entering the city is based on the city's Inspection of Meat Products Entering the City Regulations, which were approved and promulgated by the Municipal Government on October 18, 1930, and the Finance Bureau sent personnel to deliver the regulations to the pickled meat and ham associations for compliance in November of that year. The associations have sent letters to the Finance Bureau, all with the sole purpose of requesting exemption from inspection fees. This case has been going on for two years and is not a recent occurrence. It is also not true that the difficulties of merchants are disregarded. According to Article 4 of the Inspection of Meat Products Entering the City Regulations, the original inspection fee was one yuan per 100 catties, but in June of this year, the Municipal Government issued Instruction No. 1482, reducing it to only half a yuan per 100 catties, which is sufficient proof that the Municipal Government has indeed considered the difficulties of merchants. Moreover, in practice, the inspection fee per catty is only five li, and the burden of the pickled meat and ham merchants will ultimately be passed on to the consumers. Now, the consumers are paying the inspection fee for the sake of health, so why should the pickled meat and ham merchants be so angry? Moreover, the inspection of meat products entering the city is mainly aimed at eliminating inferior products and protecting public health, which is the duty of the municipal authorities. There is no reason to obstruct the process. Furthermore, every year, not only pickled meat and ham are inspected, but also fresh meat, frozen meat, lard, sausage, liver, etc., as well as all products from pigs, cattle, and sheep that can be used for food. How can the pickled meat association guarantee that there are no plague-infected meat products mixed in? Even just considering pickled meat, how can the association guarantee that plague-infected meat is not made into pickled meat elsewhere? If it is said that the pickled meat merchants will not approve the import of inferior goods, then how can it be guaranteed that the inferior goods will not be sold to the citizens? Based on the above, if public health is the premise, there is no reason to oppose the inspection of meat products entering the city. Pickled meat is a major category of meat products entering the city, and inspection is especially necessary to eliminate inferior goods and protect public health. Because the sales area is wide, it is easy for inferior goods to be mixed in, which can harm the health of consumers, and the crisis is the greatest. 2. The original letter states that the municipal authorities disregard public opinion and act arbitrarily, and they will not hesitate to make any sacrifices, etc. Municipal facilities are based on the principle of protecting the greatest happiness of the greatest number of citizens. The inspection of meat products entering the city is aimed at protecting the health of those who eat meat products entering the city. In this city, excluding vegetarians and those with religious reasons or poor children, there are at least 2 million people who eat meat products entering the city. Should the meat products that harm health not be removed for them? If there is no inspection, the safety of more than 2 million people who eat meat products entering the city will be sacrificed. Implementing inspection, then the pickled meat merchants will also be protected, and there is no sacrifice to be made. It is considered arbitrary to not understand the truth, disregard the public interest, and insist on one's own way, or to oppose it for no reason. Whether the city should inspect meat products entering the city in terms of reason and public interest is the key point that should be recognized. If you do not deny the principle that the city should seek the happiness of the greatest number of citizens, then why should you oppose the promotion of public health protection with the private views of a small group? And why should you use the threat of making any sacrifices to oppose the promotion of public health protection? This is not what an enlightened citizen and a legitimate organization should do. It is hoped that the association will reflect on this. 3. The original letter states that Shandong is the main source of pickled pork, and the slaughter tax and inspection are strict there. In fact, pickled pork is of good quality and has already been inspected, so there is no need for further inspection, etc. Before the competent health administrative agencies in each place of origin have formally notified this city, it cannot be said that this city does not need to inspect again, because there is no record to support it. The effectiveness of this city's laws and regulations should not be shaken. This is the normal course of the rule of law, and all administrative agencies and various organizations should follow it together. 4. The original letter states that foreign goods are taxed very simply and cheaply, so this repeated inspection is tantamount to a disguised method of blocking domestic products and encouraging foreign goods, etc. The simple and cheap taxation of foreign goods is due to the bias of unequal treaties, which is a great regret that all Chinese people feel deeply. However, the nature of donations and taxes is different from that of handling fees. The inspection fee is a type of handling fee and cannot be discussed in the same breath. Now, considering it from the perspective of commercial trade, the ham association should not forget the painful history of ham exports being squeezed out. In the past, other countries squeezed out the import of Chinese ham, and the only argument was that it had not been inspected by a qualified veterinarian and might harm health. If Chinese food strives to meet hygiene standards everywhere, it is also a way to strive for self-improvement. If foreign goods are protected by unequal treaties and the taxes are low, it should not be said that the hygiene of domestic goods that are prone to harm need not be inspected, and handling fees must be exempted. It is like choking on food and giving up eating. How can we compete in today's world where the fittest survive? The reason why inspection fees must be collected to cover office expenses is that public finances are insufficient, so we rely on the support of more than 2 million people who eat meat products entering the city to make things happen. The association is stuck in appearances and has this misunderstanding of putting the cart before the horse. Letting go of all food that is prone to harm is definitely not a good way to encourage domestic products and block foreign goods. Moreover, if domestic food is not subject to hygiene regulations, foreign merchants can use it as an excuse and promote how hygienic their foreign goods are in order to achieve their economic aggression strategy. The association can observe the food sold into our country and see if there is anyone who does not promote how hygienic their food is. It is hoped that the association will reflect on this. 5. The original letter states that pickled pork is pickled in salt in a salt vat and cannot produce microorganisms, so it is definitely safe, etc. If plague-infected meat is pickled in salt, even if the bacteria have been killed, the toxins excreted by the bacteria may not be completely eliminated, and those who eat it may still suffer from food poisoning. Therefore, it cannot be said that all pickled meat is hygienically safe, and the pickling method cannot be used as a guarantee that plague-infected meat is safe. 6. The original letter states that there are many things in society that harm public health, but they are not actively cleaned up. Instead, they want to impose repeated inspections and fees on pickled pork, which is safe in both fact and custom, etc. The pickling method is not a guarantee that plague-infected meat will not be mixed in, and it is not a guarantee that plague-infected meat can be considered safe once it is pickled. This has been explained in detail in the previous article, so it goes without saying that the previous misunderstandings and misinterpretations in fact and custom are not sufficient to be used as a reason to oppose inspection. As for saying that there are many things that harm public health, the association can list them in detail and report them for investigation and rectification. You cannot say that there are other things that harm public health, so there is no need to inspect meat products entering the city either. If everyone shirks responsibility, nothing will be accomplished. This is not a reason to demand the cessation of inspection of meat products entering the city. According to the letter, it is appropriate to reply, hoping that you will investigate, inform the association, and no longer adhere to prejudices and work together to promote public health in this city. I hope for this."

League of Nations Report

Phenomenon That Should Exist Amidst the Severe National Crisis

Shen Society's Report to Be Published Tomorrow

The Shanghai Shen Society, an organization composed of prominent figures in the journalism field and professors from various universities, specializing in the study of international and diplomatic issues, has, in light of the publication of the League of Nations Investigation Commission's report, and the limited number of Chinese and English copies printed by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, while the demand from all sides is very high, made a special effort to rush-print a Chinese version first, and compile world opinion of more than 10,000 words, attached to the report for reference. The society's declaration and pre-order and wholesale methods are published below:

Shen Society Declaration: The League of Nations Investigation Commission's report is what the League of Nations will use to resolve the issue of the Three Northeastern Provinces.

If the League of Nations resolves it well, the Sino-Japanese dispute can be resolved, and there is a glimmer of hope for world peace. If it is not resolved well, not only will the Sino-Japanese dispute intensify, but it may also lead to a second world war. Therefore, the League of Nations Investigation Commission's report is of great and immense importance. The survival of the Three Northeastern Provinces is closely related to the fate of our nation's people, so is this investigation report not worthy of everyone's attention? Moreover, those who study this report must observe the attitudes of the Chinese and Japanese governments and people, and the opinions of various countries in the world, before they can predict what kind of effect this report will have in the future. Therefore, an appendix of opinions from all sides is added. In short, whether the national crisis can be resolved depends entirely on the outcome of this report. The people of the country should not ignore it.

Pre-Orders Crowd the Place: The society has printed this important book in three days with great determination and unlimited sacrifice, which is no easy task. The first edition is only 5,000 copies, and it is feared that those who buy it after publication will be eager to buy it, and those who arrive later will inevitably regret it. Therefore, from yesterday (15th), it entrusted the Shen Bao newspaper office on Sanma Road and the Xinwen Bao newspaper to start selling pre-orders, charging only four corners of the ocean for each copy. After this news was released, the doors of the two newspaper offices were crowded from morning to night yesterday, with people rushing to buy the pre-order vouchers. It is estimated that 1,954 vouchers were sold in one day, and most of the buyers were young people. From this, it can be seen that the people of the country already know the seriousness of the issue of the Three Northeastern Provinces, and the League of Nations report is really too related to our country. The two newspaper offices will continue to sell today and will stop at 12:30 noon tomorrow. At 4:00 pm, the books can be picked up at the original sales location.

Purchases from Other Ports: The society is also aware that there must be countless readers in other ports who are eagerly waiting to read the contents of the report as soon as possible. The society decided that after the book is published tomorrow afternoon, it must take out 1,000 copies and immediately send them to Nanjing, Hangzhou, Beiping, Tianjin, Hankou, Hong Kong, and Guangzhou, entrusting major bookstores to sell them. Other ports are welcome to wholesale. The society has rushed to print the second batch, which will be published in three to five days. All wholesale orders must be paid in cash, at least 100 copies, calculated at a 30% discount, plus one yuan for postage to show preferential treatment. Those who wish to wholesale can send a letter to the distribution department of the Shen Society at Guohua Advertising Company, No. 280 Shandong Road, Shanghai. Retail readers can purchase from the Shanghai Shen Society (address as above), calculated at 95% of the postage.

Chinese and English Versions: The Chinese version translated by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is already faithful and accurate, but there is an even greater need for Chinese and English bilingual editions to be compared with each other. Therefore, a Chinese and English bilingual edition is also being printed at the same time and is being proofread. It will also be published in the shortest possible time and will be announced later.

The Yarn and Cloth Exchange Case 165

The Second Instance Was Heard Yesterday

Both Sides Made Detailed Statements

Clients of the Yarn and Cloth Exchange, such as Sha Weiyi, sued the exchange in the First Special District Court for illegally resolving all clients' futures trading on February 9, resulting in huge losses. Judge Yang Peng ruled that the resolution of the Yarn and Cloth Exchange on February 9 was invalid. The exchange did not accept the original judgment and appealed. Yesterday afternoon at 1:30 pm, the president of the High Court, Hu Yigu, personally heard the case. Gao Shoutian of the Yarn and Cloth Exchange, along with lawyers Liu Chongyou, Zhang Shizhao, Wang Fushang, Chen Zhongyin, etc., arrived in court around 1:00 pm. The defendants Sha Weiyi, Fu Zidong, Wang Junbai, Ming Jingheng, Chen Rongcai, Wang Shengchu, etc., and lawyers Shi Ying, Tao Jiachun, Yao Xichen, Zhang Zhengxue, and more than ten people who participated in the lawsuit, such as Wang Guanxian, arrived in court one after another to await the hearing. President Hu took a seat in the Second Civil Court. First, the plaintiff's lawyer stated that the first instance was lost. On the appellant's side, it was believed that the original judgment's reasoning was insufficient, and the original judge did not fully understand the Exchange Law. Therefore, they appealed, and explained the reasons for the suspension of trading due to the war. Then, the defendant's lawyers Shi Ying, Tao Jiachun, Zhang Zhengxue, etc., denied the resolution of the previous meeting of the Exchange Council because the number of attendees did not meet the quorum, and proved that there was still trading of spot yarn at the time, but the exchange forcibly closed other people's trading. It is difficult to recognize in reason and law. Both sides made detailed statements and corrections. Until 5:30 pm, it was too late, so it was announced that the date would be changed to start the debate.

Assassination of Wu Guangzong Case 166

The First Special Court Rules That Judgment Should Be Based on Existing Charges

The case should then be transferred to the Municipal Public Security Bureau

Henan natives Song Jiande, Wu Guigui, Zhang Shaoliang, and Huzhou native Yao Jiechen, committed robbery at the Changxing Coal Mine Bureau in Zhejiang Province last November, fatally shooting the bureau's police chief, surnamed Lu, and stealing over 5,000 silver dollars and over ten firearms. Recently, Li Nianyuan, the detective chief of the Second Regiment of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Team, along with detective Yao Bailin, and collaborating with Liu Junqing, a Chinese detective from the Old Zha station of the Public Concession, and Bao Tangyu, a detective, apprehended them at hotels such as the Juelu Hotel. Four pistols bearing the seal of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau were confiscated. They were brought to the First Special Court for interrogation and detention. Subsequently, Song and others confessed that the assassination of Wu Guangzong, the director of the Hydrographic Office of the Ministry of Navy, and the robbery at No. 1040 Wuzhou Road were committed by them and Zhou Mingshan. Zhou Mingshan (also known as Zhou Asi) is now serving as a detective in the Second Regiment of the Zhejiang Security Team. The police arrested Zhou, as previously reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Feng De, the presiding judge of the criminal division of the First Special Court, continued the interrogation in criminal court No. 1. First, Ru Baoyi, the police lawyer, stated that the police were only charging the defendants with robbery and violating Article 1 of the Regulations for the Suppression of Military Firearms. Regarding the assassination of Wu Guangzong, although the police suspected the defendants, they did not bring charges and would leave it to the competent authorities to handle. However, the Public Security Bureau has now detained Zhang Changlin, who is also a principal offender in the Wuzhou Road robbery case, and the cases should be tried together. He requested the court to send a document to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to bring Zhang for joint interrogation and requested another extension of the hearing. Zhan Jifeng, a legal counsel, also represented the Municipal Public Security Bureau in court and requested that the defendants be handed over. Lawyer Zhan stated that criminal cases should be prosecuted based on the severity of the crime, and the most serious crime should be prosecuted first. The case of the defendants plotting to kill Wu Guangzong is the most serious, and the law allows for the death penalty. The robbery case brought by the police can only be punished with imprisonment. Therefore, the murder case is more serious than the robbery case. Thus, the case should be handed over to the Public Security Bureau for investigation and prosecution first. Moreover, Wu Guangzong was an incumbent official, and the defendants dared to assassinate him, which is obviously a major event. If the investigation is delayed, it would greatly impede the investigation, which should be noted by the court. Lawyer Ru immediately stated that the police are willing to assist the Public Security Bureau, but since the police have already brought charges in this case, a judgment should be made first on the existing charges before the Public Security Bureau takes over the case, in accordance with legal procedure. The representative of the Zhejiang Security Team also requested that the defendants be transferred to Zhejiang. Judge Feng declared that since the police had already brought charges in this case, a judgment should be made first on the existing charges before they could be transferred. Furthermore, the assassination of Wu Guangzong occurred in Shanghai, and for the convenience of investigation, the case should be transferred to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation. In the future, when the bureau sends the case to the local court, it must notify the Security Team whether the case can be transferred to the local court of Zhejiang Province for adjudication. Thus, the case was adjourned for another hearing, and the defendants were returned to custody.

After the Murderer Chen Tugeng Escaped 167

Severely Punish the Guards

One Fat, One Thin, Each With a Photograph

Such Negligence is Truly Blameworthy

The Shanghai Local Court Detention Center had murderer Chen Tugeng and gambling offender Chen Tugeng enter the detention center successively. As the sentence of the gambling offender Chen Tugeng had been completed, he was released under substituted execution. The murderer Chen Tugeng was then substituted, and escaped. This was reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that after reading the report, the President of the Local Court, Chief Prosecutor, and others immediately went to the detention center to investigate and found it to be true. They immediately handed over Bao Fuchen, the clerk in charge of receiving and dispatching, and Li Yamin, the head of the guard, to the prosecutor for investigation. When the detention center receives and dispatches prisoners, it should first inspect the defendant's photograph. The head of the guard should hand it over to the clerk for further verification, and inquire about the age, origin, and cause of the case, and compare it with the case file before releasing or receiving them. Chen Tugeng both have photographs, and the murderer Chen Tugeng is fat, while the gambling offender Chen Tugeng is thin. This kind of negligence is truly blameworthy, and the escape has been for many days. Therefore, those with specific responsibilities in the detention center are all responsible. Therefore, Bao and Li were ordered to provide reliable guarantors and were given a deadline to recapture the prisoner, otherwise, they would be punished together.

Alas

Two Young Men Drown Themselves 168

Names and Ages Cannot Be Investigated

The Reasons for Suicide Are Difficult to Ascertain

Over the past two days, two young men have successively committed suicide by jumping into the Huangpu River from sampans. Both were not rescued and died in the river. Their names, ages, and reasons for suicide are unknown. The circumstances are described below:

A Loud Cry At 10:40 p.m. the night before last, a young man in a Western suit came to the wharf of the New Customs House on the Bund of Hankou Road. He looked around on the wharf and hesitated for a moment. He then hired sampan No. 68, saying that he wanted to cross to Pudong. The sampan operator, Pa Gencai, thought he was an ordinary passenger, so he did not pay attention and immediately moved the sampan away from the shore, gradually heading towards Pudong. The moon was bright, and the river was like a mirror. When the sampan reached the center of the river, the young man suddenly stood up from the cabin, shouted loudly, and jumped into the river to commit suicide. When the sampan operator, Xin Gencai, saw this, he was shocked and tried his best to rescue him with a bamboo rake. However, the angry waves were merciless, and the man was gone. Xin had no choice but to bring the empty boat to the Customs Water Police Station to report the situation and leave. The body of the deceased has not been found as of last night.

Emerging Twice Yesterday at 8:00 a.m., a young man wearing a light-colored long robe and speaking with a Ningbo accent also went to the New Customs House wharf and hired sampan No. 1395 to cross to the Jiangmatou in Pudong. When the sampan reached the center of the river, the man also jumped into the river to commit suicide. At this time, the sampan operator, Dai Genyou, was panicked and saw the jumper emerging twice, but did not attempt to rescue him. Instead, he turned around and tried to escape. Wang Haiquan, a detective from the Customs Water Police Station, was also sitting on the sampan in front of them. Upon learning that someone had jumped into the river, he quickly ordered the operator of his own sampan to turn back and try to rescue him. However, they were too far away from each other, and by the time they arrived at the scene, the person had already sunk and disappeared. Detective Wang believed that the sampan operator, Dai Genyou, had missed the opportunity to rescue the deceased, which was tantamount to causing death by negligence, and that he had fled in hopes of escaping punishment, which was extremely hateful. He immediately detained Dai and the boat at the police station. After questioning by the police chief, the sampan was detained at the police station, and Dai was handed over to the original detective to be sent to the Local Court for questioning.

Robbery Case on North Henan Road

Twelve More Robbers Apprehended 169

Rickshaw Driver Had Bad Intentions

Owner Behaved Extravagantly

The home of Wang Shaofu, a Ningbo native, at No. 123 Taoyuanfang, North Henan Road, was invaded by several robbers at around 8:00 a.m. the day before yesterday. They brandished guns to silence any outcry, and three robbers went upstairs to start searching. One robber stood guard at the entrance. Subsequently, a neighboring woman reported it to the Chinese police on guard nearby and telephoned the Hongkou Police Station in charge, who dispatched all Chinese and foreign detectives to surround the area. The robbers opened fire to resist arrest. As a result, two robbers were shot dead on the spot by the Chinese and foreign detectives. Two others were also severely injured and sent to the hospital for treatment. The bodies of the dead robbers were transported to the Forensic Examination Office on Philen Road for examination. This has been reported in detail. However, two foreign detectives were also injured in the incident and are now being treated at the Public Hospital. Afterwards, Shen Rongli, the Chinese detective chief in charge of the case, along with detectives Zhang Gui, Bao Shuji, and Cantonese detective Feng Qi, apprehended twelve more accomplices: Zheng Guangzong, Wang Acai, Lu Jinsheng, Zhang Aer, Kong Rongsheng, Yue Meisheng, Wu Peigen, Ding Guirong, Wei Baoquan, Chen Yinfa, Fan Jinyuan, and Zhu Amao, at the Baohe Hotel at No. 200 Guangdong Road, No. 714 Xiamen Road, Furenli on Beijing Road, and No. 18 Beiler Road in the French Concession. They were taken into custody at the police station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to Criminal Court No. 3 of the First Special District Court. Zhang Tianyin, the police lawyer, recounted the events in detail and stated that the two injured robbers, one named Jiang Huixing and the other said to be Zhu Youlong, were in the hospital and could not be brought before the court. One dead robber was named Ma Zhengxiang, and the other was surnamed Mu. However, it was discovered that the mastermind behind the case was the defendant Zhang Aer. Zhang was employed as a rickshaw driver for the victim Wang Shaofu for over ten years. Recently, he noticed that his employer often carried hundreds of dollars in cash and that his wife, Wang Shenshi, had diamond rings and other valuable diamond jewelry. He informed the fourth defendant, Wang Acai, and discussed it for a month. Wang then invited the deceased Ma Zhengxiang and others to commit the robbery yesterday. Wang admitted this to the police without denial. The defendant Kong Rongsheng was implicated by the injured robber Jiang Huixing, who said that he was the one who supplied the firearms for the case. The other defendants denied the charges to the police. Therefore, he requested a postponement for investigation. He then presented two pistols for inspection. Then, the victim Wang Shenshi, the maid Cao Wangshi, and the neighboring woman Zhang Yeshi testified about the events. Wang Acai was questioned and confessed that a month ago, Zhang Aer came and said that there was something he could do and asked if he had any friends. He asked what it was, and Zhang Aer said that his employer, surnamed Wang, often had hundreds of dollars and diamond jewelry with him. He initially ignored it, but a few days ago, Zhang invited him again, and he discussed it with the deceased Ma Zhengxiang and agreed to commit the robbery. When questioned, Zhang Aer denied being the mastermind, saying that his employer treated him well, and he would never have such bad intentions. Kong Rongsheng testified that the injured robber Jiang Huixing, nicknamed Jiang Xiaoningbo, had committed a kidnapping case four years ago, and he had notified the police, who arrested him and sent him to the court for punishment. After serving his sentence, he was released. He held a grudge and falsely accused him of supplying the firearms. He hired Lawyer Jiang to defend him for a year. After Judge Shen Bingrong questioned the other defendants, he ordered them to be returned to custody for further investigation. Regarding the two dead robbers, the court appointed Prosecutor Guo Wei to inspect the bodies at the site at around 9:00 a.m. yesterday. He examined the two dead unidentified men and determined that they had been shot and killed by the police on the spot while resisting arrest. The two bodies were handed over to the Pushan Villa for burial. Three recovered pistols were handed over to the police firearms department for safekeeping and verification.

Continued Loan of American Wheat 172

The Ministry of Finance Sent Yang Ge to Shanghai Yesterday to Continue Negotiations

The Shanghai News Agency reports that the second loan of American wheat by the National Government was officially signed by the US Consul General in Shanghai, Mr. Ke Yinhang, and Military Affairs Committee Chairman Chiang Kai-shek at Chiang's villa in Lushan on the 4th of this month, as per the previous contract between the two parties. It is now learned that the agreement signed by the US and China in Lushan on the 4th was a draft agreement, not a formal contract. Finance Minister Song Ziwen has appointed American advisor Yang Ge to come to Shanghai yesterday to continue negotiations with the US representatives stationed in Shanghai. The details are recorded below:

Negotiation Process The motivation for this second loan of American wheat by the National Government came from the American Finance Rehabilitation Corporation, because this year's bumper harvest of agricultural products in various parts of the United States is more than three times higher than in previous years, resulting in a surplus of grain that cannot be sold. In August, it took the initiative to telegraph the Chinese government to negotiate a continuation of the loan. After Finance Minister Song Ziwen convened a meeting with all parties related to civil food to study the matter, it was deemed feasible. A telegram was immediately sent back to the American Finance Rehabilitation Corporation for further negotiations, and at the same time, the issue and the results of the meeting were telegraphed to Chiang Kai-shek in Lushan for final decision. Subsequently, Chiang replied by telegram, approving the request and telegraphed Finance Minister Song Ziwen to invite US Consul General Ke Yinhang stationed in Shanghai to Lushan for a face-to-face discussion of everything. The US and China then held a meeting at Chiang's villa in Lushan on October 4 to discuss the continued loan and sign a draft agreement. As for the formal contract, it still needs to be negotiated by the US advisor Yang Gen of the Ministry of Finance and the Shanghai representative of the American Finance Rehabilitation Corporation before it can be signed.

Yang Ge Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Yang Ge, the American advisor to the Ministry of Finance, arrived in Shanghai from Beijing yesterday by order of Song to negotiate with the US representative stationed in Shanghai on the issue of continuing the loan of American wheat. According to Yang, the total amount of the National Government's second loan of American wheat is about 450,000 tons, worth 12 million US dollars (approximately 50 million Chinese dollars). Although the draft agreement has been signed, the formal contract still needs to be negotiated and signed. As for the method of shipping it to China in batches, the two parties have also agreed that the first batch is scheduled to start loading and shipping to China at the beginning of next month.

Settlement of Disputes in the Brewing Industry 174

Both Parties Signed Seven Conditions

The brewing industry in this city experienced labor-management disputes due to workers' demands for improved treatment, which were mediated by the Social Affairs Bureau several times without result. Finally, three draft plans were proposed, and opinions gradually converged. Yesterday morning at 10:00 a.m., the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau convened labor and management representatives to the bureau again for mediation. Labor representatives Wang Bingkui and Shen Guomin, management representatives Zhu Qingtang and Fang Zhongheng, and Municipal Party Headquarters representative Li Weixiong attended. The chairman, Tan Peiyan, of the Third Section of the Social Affairs Bureau, immediately agreed to sign seven conditions and announced the settlement. The original text is recorded below: (1) The workshop recognizes the Shanghai Brewing Industry Professional Trade Union as having the right to represent all members (hereinafter referred to as workers). (2) If there are vacancies in the workshop, members of the trade union should be hired first. This shall not apply if the trade union members do not have the required qualifications. If non-members are hired, the management shall be responsible for ordering them to join the union. (3) When the trade union holds a representative conference approved by the Party and government authorities, the management shall not hinder the representatives sent by each workshop from attending. If they are late or leave early for reasons, the trade union shall inform the management in writing, and their wages may be deducted as appropriate. (4) The management shall increase the salary of each person by six jiao of silver dollars per month. (5) Labor and management shall assist each other in the future. If there are disputes that cannot be resolved by both parties, they shall submit them to the higher-level authorities for handling. (6) All treatments in each workshop shall be handled according to the usual practice. (7) The management shall comply with the treatments that conform to the Factory Law.
