Liu Haisu Art Exhibition Opened Yesterday

Mayor Wu Personally Delivered the Opening Speech

More Than Two Hundred Works on Display

The Liu Haisu European Travel Works Exhibition, organized by the Shanghai Municipal Government, opened at the Chen Yingshi Memorial Hall on Beijing Road at 10:00 a.m. yesterday. Over two hundred people attended, including Mayor Wu, Ye Gongchuo, Li Jishen and his wife, Pan Gongzhan, Chen Qicai, Wu Kaisheng, Wang Jiyuan, Shu Xincheng, Xie Gongzhan, and Liu Haisu and his wife. The details are recorded separately below:

Ceremony Order (1) Playing music, (2) All stand at attention, (3) Sing the Party song, (4) Pay the highest respect to the national flag, Party flag, and Sun Yat-sen's portrait, (5) The chairman respectfully reads Sun Yat-sen's will, (6) Silence, (7) The mayor delivers the opening speech, (8) The representative of the Ministry of Education delivers a speech (The Ministry of Education originally sent Xiao Youmei, the president of the National Conservatory of Music, to deliver a speech, but Xiao was unable to attend due to temporary affairs), (9) Ye Gongchuo, Chen Qicai, Pan Gongzhan, Wu Kaisheng, Shu Xincheng, Li Jishen, Xie Gongzhan, and others deliver speeches in succession, (10) Liu Haisu delivers a thank-you speech, and the ceremony is announced in the sound of music.

Mayor's Speech Mayor Wu said in his opening speech yesterday, "Today is the opening day of the Liu Haisu European Travel Works Exhibition held by the Shanghai Municipal Government. Thank you all for your presence and support. At the same time, I would like to thank Mr. Liu Haisu for bringing all his works from his European travels to be displayed here. The municipal government feels very grateful. Although it is the first time for a local government in China to hold a private works exhibition, we dare not claim the reputation of initiating it in Shanghai. The government should encourage and promote works that express the spirit of the country and the nation. However, in recent years, China has been busy reorganizing its internal affairs, relieving natural disasters, and resisting foreign insults, so it has had no time to pay attention to this. Shanghai is the center of Chinese culture, and the municipal government should take this opportunity to promote and encourage it. Mr. Liu Haisu's art does not need to be praised with the best adjectives. His works can tell us his expression of society and the country. This is the meaning of the Municipal Government holding the Liu Haisu European Travel Works Exhibition."

A Glimpse of the Painting Studio The works exhibited by Liu Haisu are divided into three parts. The first part is the works before his European travel, which are displayed in the Lake Society Hall. The second part is the works from his European travels, which are displayed in the Chen Yingshi Memorial Hall. The third part is the new works after his return from Europe, which are displayed in the upstairs hall of the Yingshi Memorial Hall, with a total of 225 pieces of various sizes. The most brilliant are a few of Liu's copies of "Dante and Virgil" and "Slaughter" in Paris. It is said that the exhibition period is 17 days.

China Science Society 177

Commemorating the Great Inventor Edison

Publication of Commemorative Special Issue

Measures for Commemorative Award

The great inventor American Edison passed away on October 18 last year. On the occasion of the anniversary, the monthly journal "Science" published by the China Science Society will publish a special commemorative issue for the anniversary of Edison's death this month (No. 10, 16th year), listing more than ten articles, covering almost all of the life and deeds of Edison and his contribution to modern civilization, and inserting many photos of Edison from his youth to his old age, which is especially rare. At the end of last year, the Society initiated the raising of the Edison Memorial Award Fund to reward young people in our country who are engaged in invention and to commemorate Edison Liu permanently. The amount raised by the end of last year has reached 1,800 yuan. The Council of the Society resolved five articles of the award-giving method the day before yesterday, and publicly elected Ren Hongjun, Yan Renguang, and Huang Boqiao as members of the Award Committee. The award-giving method is recorded as follows: China Science Society Edison Memorial Award-Giving Method (1) This award is a gold medal with a cash prize of 100 yuan. (2) The scope of the award is limited to inventions in applied science. (3) The Council of the Society shall elect three experts to form the Edison Memorial Award Committee to preside over the review matters. (4) Any young person of the Republic of China who has a new invention in applied science shall submit his new invention and its statement to the Review Committee for review by the introduction of two members. (5) This award will be held once a year, and the committee will recommend one or several of the best achievements from those engaged in invention in China to the Council for approval. However, if there is no suitable candidate this year, it may be extended to the next year for distribution.

Municipal Garden Farm

Cheap Distribution of Famous Varieties of Chrysanthemums 178

The Municipal Garden Farm, set up by the Social Affairs Bureau of this city, has natural scenery and abundant flowers and trees. Although the farm has been affected by the current situation in recent years and its expenses have been strained, the work of the farm has not been delayed in the slightest. The farm has made considerable achievements in the collection, cultivation, and improvement of flowers and trees. The farm has a particularly rich collection of chrysanthemums, with more than 400 varieties and 6,000 to 7,000 pots. It also has other flowers and trees. If you need them, you can contact them or make an appointment. The farm is located in Donggou, Pudong, facing the sea and bordering the river, which is a beautiful garden resort. Those who want to visit can take the municipal ferry from the Copper Man Pier on the Bund of Nanjing Road to Donggou and get off the boat.

Machine Union Association

Page 16

Meeting of the Land and Housing Supervisory Committee 179

Resolution to Organize Two Research Committees

The Shanghai Machinery and National Goods Factories Joint Association held a joint meeting of the supervisory committee on the afternoon of the previous day (14th) at 6 PM at the Central Vegetable Society on Fourth Road. Over ten people attended, including Ji Jiannan, Zhu Wenqi, Lu Fengzhu, Dong Zhexian, Chen Xingwu, and Song Peidao. Zhu Wenqi was publicly elected as chairman. First, Ji Jiannan reported on the significance of the proposals for the meeting, stating that the association's affairs were mainly managed by the executive committee. However, the number of executive committee members was small, and each had their own expertise, which was a regrettable shortcoming in the full expression of the association's affairs. In order to promote the association's business, it seemed necessary to gather the strength of many people to operate together, cooperate fully, and benefit from collective wisdom and concerted efforts. In view of this, the association specially proposed at this meeting the organization of a National Goods Movement Committee, a Labor Dispute Research Committee, a Personnel Issues Committee, and a Special Incident Investigation Committee to promote the development of the association's affairs, and elaborated on the significance, tasks, and necessity of each committee. The chairman then submitted it for discussion. Subsequently, Lu Fengzhu, Bao Juting, Chen Xingwu, Wang Xingyao, Yang Weiyin, and others successively expressed their opinions. After the chairman summarized the opinions of the meeting, he submitted it for a vote. It was resolved to merge the National Goods Movement Committee and the Special Incident Investigation Committee into the National Goods Movement Committee, and to merge the Labor Dispute Research Committee and the Personnel Issues Committee into the Factory Affairs Research Committee. In addition to the members attending the meeting, eight non-attending members were publicly elected to form the committee together, and those with special research and interest were solicited to participate freely. Zhu Zhenhan was designated as the convener of the National Goods Movement Committee, and Ji Jiannan was designated as the convener of the Factory Affairs Research Committee. All organizational methods and business plans would be reported to the Executive and Supervisory Committees after being discussed by the conveners and all members.

Post-Accident Meeting of the Da Yun Steamer 182

Since the Da Yun accident, Du Shaoru, the manager of Yongyu Company, convened an emergency meeting of the board of directors and supervisors yesterday (the 15th) to discuss the aftermath. Here is a record of the situation: Manager Du Shaoru reported that the company received a telegram yesterday, the 13th, at 2 PM, stating that the Da Yun had sunk in Baopu. He immediately dispatched the Dalian steamer to the scene of the accident to investigate the situation. After the Dalian steamer went, according to the report of the business director Du Yuzan, the accident was caused by the 700-foot-long stone dike in Baopu. At that time, the tide was rising and bursting. The dike water rushed south, and the ship was alongside the dock. The ship's cables were tightened, causing the water to rush south, and the ship tilted north. At the same time, when the passengers were on board and the ship was not yet docked, they flocked to the north side, causing a tragedy. Fortunately, the Yongzhou steamer and barges rescued more than a hundred people, and fifty or sixty people drowned. Whether the shipowner and others neglected their duties has been sent to the county for questioning by the Fourth District Public Security Bureau. On the one hand, more than twenty salvage workers were hired to salvage the corpses and prepare coffins for burial. The local administrative organs have notified the families of the victims to collect them separately and take care of the passengers' cargo. The competent authorities have also been reported separately by the company. In addition, the shipping schedule was adjusted, and the company's Dalian steamer was dispatched to replace the shift. For the salvage of the ship's hull, contact was made with the Wheelock & Yison Shipyard, but the salvage cost exceeded the ship's cost and no agreement was reached. It is planned to contact other companies. If the salvage cost is appropriate, it will be reported again. Director Ji Youshi stood up and said that the cost at the time was more than 100,000 yuan. After ten years of operation, according to the current market price, what is the value of the ship? The manager replied that the shipping vessels have a depreciation of 20 years, which is considered fully depreciated. This ship has been operating for ten years and is only worth 70,000 to 80,000 yuan. Whether it can be salvaged or re-ordered should be decided by the shareholders' meeting. The meeting adjourned at 5 PM. The reporter also spoke with Manager Du Shaoru as follows: (Q) What is the capital of your company? (A) 180,000 yuan. (Q) How many ships does the company have? (A) The Da Yun and the Dalian. (Q) How is the business situation usually? (A) Only official profits have been left over the years. (Q) How much is the loss this time? (A) In the range of 70,000 to 80,000 yuan. (Q) Are there any compensations for the bereaved families and crew members? (A) This unfortunate incident is very regrettable. (Q) Will the steamer be salvaged? (A) The board of directors and supervisors will decide to publish a tender. (Q) Do you have any relationship with the establishment of various companies? (A) The companies founded by my brothers are all of a limited nature. For example, the Datong Yarn Factory only spent about 10,000 yuan on Huayi. The nature of other companies is separate and has no relationship.

Arrest of Xu Peiwen and others who plotted to set up gambling dens

In the area where Zhabei in Shanghai is both Chinese and foreign, some unscrupulous Chinese and Japanese people have been privately setting up gambling dens, enticing the ignorant to enter the dens, which is harmful to society. Robbery on Route Saypo 185

A Bloodshed Caused by Demanding Clothes 186

Shen Laobeizi Opens Fire and Chops with an Ax

Neighbor Hua Guangsheng Injured in the Face

Huang Xiaojianzi, a coppersmith from Jiangbei, 31 years old, lives in the back building of No. 16 Xiangshan Road, Xiangyan Bridge. He is friendly with his fellow villager Shen Laobeizi (30 years old). However, Shen is a vagrant. A month ago, Shen borrowed a wool clip gown and a single long shirt from Huang because he was short of money and paid the pawnshop. Ten days ago, Huang was in need of the wool clip gown to keep warm because the weather was getting colder. And recently, Shen has been working at a flower meeting and his finances have improved slightly. So he asked Shen to redeem the clothes. Who knew that after meeting, Shen became angry and embarrassed, and spoke rudely. An argument arose, which was resolved by friends. When leaving, Huang threatened Shen Laobeizi, saying that if he did not see the redeemed clothes, the flower meeting would have to be reported to the police. At about 4 AM yesterday, Shen gathered a few people and broke into Huang's residence, firing at Huang. Four shots were fired, one in the chest, the bullet exiting from the back, one in the left shoulder, one in the right leg, and one in the right wrist. Two ax wounds were inflicted on the right leg, and the wounds were very deep. Blood gushed out like a spring, and he became unconscious. When the bullets were flying, a stray bullet injured the face of his neighbor Hua Guangsheng, who sells fruit. Fortunately, the injury was light, slightly scraping his face. The murderers, seeing that their goal had been achieved, fled in a swarm. The injured were immediately taken to Tongren Hospital by the co-residents for treatment. It is said that the injuries are serious and his life is in danger.

Business Community Asks for Lighthouse Construction 193

Representatives from the Shanghai Timber Industry Association, Shu Jiliang; the Shanghai Sandboat Trade Association, Zhu Ziqian; and the Shanghai Flower Trade Association, Cheng Xifu, and others, submitted a request to Luo, the Customs Commissioner of the Jianghai Customs; Tang, the Customs Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs; and Hu Chengyun, the Director of the Nanshi Branch of the Jianghai Customs, requesting the construction of a lighthouse to secure the ships because the old pole lights had collapsed and the journey was dangerous. The city of Nanhui, Nicheng, is located on the coast, and the southeast Huijiao is opposite to Yangshan. All the sailing boats going back and forth must pass through this road, and the tide is turbulent and the situation is extremely dangerous. And the local people here have always been tough. If a ship is stranded by the tide, they will definitely plunder it until the ship's goods are gone. Therefore, navigators are afraid of it. During the Qing Dynasty, Wang Yuzhou, a gentleman of the town, reported the above situation to the county magistrate, who reported it to the superiors. They allocated the army and stationed them in the Tianhou Palace for protection. And Tu Dong Sun Xiaopu and wood merchant Qiu Zhuxi discussed and proposed to build a light pole at the most important location to be the standard for ships to travel back and forth at night. It has been standing for more than ten years. However, because the pole is limited and the light does not reach far, ships sailing at night are still unable to travel safely. Therefore, the number of ships encountering danger has been heard from time to time. Traders and merchants have suffered losses. It is sincerely hoped that you will be sympathetic to the difficulties of the merchants, and there will be no minutiae. Therefore, we jointly request you to review and approve the appointment of a commissioner to build a lighthouse at the most important location so that ships traveling back and forth can see the bright stars early in the morning in foggy days and dark nights, and know how to avoid dangerous waters and dangerous shoals. Then the benefits for the shipping merchants will be infinite. Issued on October 15, 21st year of the Republic of China.

Weather Report 202

The Xujiahui Observatory issued a weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday, stating that the morning will be sunny and cloudy with light fog. The wind direction in the coastal area and the slightly northern area will be uncertain, or will suddenly turn northwest. The strong winds in the Taiwan Strait come from the north to the northeast. There is a gentle cyclone on the coast of Annam. The center of the windy point is 6 o'clock within 120 miles of the intersection of 15 degrees north latitude and 113 degrees east longitude, moving west, and the wind force is unknown. Also, in the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the city was 78.8 and the lowest was 53.2. On the same day last year, the highest was 79.5 and the lowest was 50.9.

Sayings of Elder Ma Xiangbo at Ninety-Three 203

From Liu Haisu to Chinese and Western Painting 204

— ·Jing·Ji

"Respect the real ground, respect the void spirit; using firewood to pass on the fire, who is the master and who is the guest?"

This is a poem that Old Man Xiang presented to Liu Haisu; because his paintings will be exhibited in this city, a letter came asking Master Ding to write a preface, and he also painted a piece himself.

Asked, how to explain "real ground" and "void spirit"?

Old Man Xiang immediately had a wonderful analogy, saying that the character 'Su' (粟) is the answer! We looked at each other for a moment, and Old Man Xiang smiled and explained it more clearly:

"Breaking down the characters to explain; the character 'Hai' (海) is the void spirit, because it only has the shape and sound of water; the character 'Su' (粟) is the real ground, like the original object. Why bother to explain it in detail! Let me talk about Chinese and Western painting at random!"

Chinese painting, with a stroke or two of description, famous artists are good at conveying the spirit; it seems to have a philosophical meaning! Mo Jing called it "divine ease". In fact, it is all empty depiction. When painting a human face, it is not necessary to have all the ears, eyes, mouth, and nose! Western painting is sometimes very strange... painting a human head, depicting a fish body... like the Egyptian sphinx; it is also called a great art. When we look at it, we don't feel any meaning!

Now Chinese and Western painting are learning from each other. It is truly "using firewood to pass on the fire"; let's see in the future, in the comparison and competition, who will be more victorious in the history of painting!

We originally wanted to ask about Mr. Haisu and nude paintings; then we thought that recent reports said that the German government had ordered a ban on nude sports, saying it was a sign of cultural decline; Old Man Xiang certainly wouldn't say complimentary words either!

Seeking Help from Others is Not as Good as Seeking Help from Yourself 205

— ·Guo·Wei·Ran

| I hope the countrymen will be keenly aware |

Seeking help from others is not as good as seeking help from yourself – this saying, although a commonplace, has a profound meaning. The root of the national character lies in reliance. When doing things in society, one must first have a backer. I ask, which administrative personnel does not have a backer? If the mountain is not high, the backing is not solid. Once the mountain collapses, the backing falls. This is what is meant by "the creeper loses its shade." If this nature is not changed, one person is not cultivated, one family is not regulated, one country is not governed, and the world is not at peace. Changing customs depends entirely on the refinement of education. Those who are responsible, why not start doing it!

"Weak countries have no diplomacy," this saying is most opposed by the high-sounding gentlemen. China is a weak country, which is undeniable. However, is it really a weak country? I believe that the strength or weakness of a country depends entirely on human effort. If you want to turn weakness into strength, it is not impossible. As the saying goes, "It is not that we cannot do it, but that we do not do it." Will China continue to be in chaos? It depends on the administrative leaders restraining themselves and recommending the worthy, and striving for the permanent happiness of the country and the nation.

The League of Nations is unreliable, everyone in China and abroad says. The League of Nations is a group of imperialists. Japan, an imperial power, is one of the five great powers. The League of Nations naturally cannot but perfunctorily deal with it. Like our great China, as if it were a numb sleeping lion, who would bother to care about you? Supporting the weak and suppressing the strong is just such a "platitude." Among nations, there is only "combination of interests," and there is no "international trust"!

"Seeking help from others is not as good as seeking help from yourself." I hope that the central government can truly wholeheartedly correct the military warlordism, concentrate political power, and concentrate the nation's talent and economy to work for national salvation by internal pacification and external resistance. Defeating Japan is the beginning of destroying the walls of all imperialists. Once Japanese imperialism collapses, there will be hope for equality in the world!

Inconceivable Revenge 206

| In the end, you're just asking for trouble |

A young master chased after a modern young lady every day, went through all kinds of hardships, and obtained the permission of both families. "She made me suffer before, now I make her suffer, to get revenge on her." As a result, the two sides broke up, and he had no choice but to take out a large sum of alimony. Unexpectedly, he recently opened an even larger silk weaving factory than before. I really admire his ability. One day I ran into him on the road and asked him the details. He said, "I was burned into a pauper by the Japanese, but now I'm still making money off of them. Alas! The revenge of a treacherous merchant." Now I see the workers of the anti-treachery group being worried all day long.

Young People in Love, Be Careful 207

— ·Cheng·Da

| Here's a deadly story for you |

In general, modern young men and women like to be in love. That's right, it's a natural psychology. But you must know that the power of love is the greatest. It can easily make you successful and happy, and it can also easily make you negative and decadent. Now there is a very good, very tortuous, and very meaningful story. This story is roughly like this... There was a college student who was initially a decadent figure, but soon he had a lover. He was excited, he worked hard, but unexpectedly good things are often hard-won, and he mistakenly thought that his lover's brother was his rival in love, and he became negative again. He was thinking of committing suicide to end his life, but his lover saved him, understood everything, and the lovers finally got married.

This story shows... (1) The only obstacles to love are "doubt" and "jealousy." (2) The success of love is not easy without going through a twist. (3) For the sake of love, one can be excited, but also not want to live. This shows how great the power of love is.

It is said that the Mingxing Film Company's new film "Love and Life" has adopted such a story. Of course, our college students will definitely rush to see it, because after seeing it, at least we can know what love is all about, and how the success of this matter is like.

Design of Cocoon Room without Pupae 208

— ·Tian·Xu·Wo·Sheng

My purpose is to make the silkworm pupae not in the cocoon, and without the consumption of silk spitting head, the silk spun by each silkworm can be completely used for normal purposes, and the cocoon baking procedure is avoided, so this design is made, which has many benefits... No silkworm nests are needed, reducing the location, first; the silkworm's feces and urine are not in the cocoon, the surface and inside are pure and clean, and the silk is not disordered, second; the pupae are not inside, the weight of the cocoon is the weight of pure silk, and the selling price is high, third; no fire baking is needed, there is no worry about moths emerging, the labor cost is reduced, the production is increased, and the quality is excellent, fourth; each room houses 150 silkworms, only three inches high, only one foot long, and about half a foot wide, slightly like an abacus, which can be stacked like a brick wall. But there is only two feet of land, about ten feet long, stacked six feet high, which can hold three hundred rooms, and each time one hundred catties of pupa-free cocoons can be collected, which is light, convenient, and suitable for women. The system is described below...

Use a two-tenths-thick board to make the walls around, one and a half inches high, seven inches wide, and twelve inches long, without a cover. The bottom is made of a four-tenths-thick board, drilled with three-tenths-inch diameter holes, ten holes vertically, and fifteen holes horizontally, shaped like a drawer inside a matchbox. Use cardboard inside to divide it into 150 square grids, each grid six tenths of an inch square. Cut thin cardboard like cigarette paper, one and a half inches wide and two and a half inches long, roll it into a cylinder on a wooden stick, without gluing it firmly, so that it can roll and stretch. Then insert this roll into each square grid, so that the inner layer becomes circular. Four legs are attached to the bottom of the box, one inch high, and the total height is only three inches. If this is prepared, the mechanized cost for every 300 rooms is only thirty to fifty yuan, and it can be used for at least a dozen years. Even if there is damage, it is only the inner cardboard, and each replacement costs only a few cents. (Note: The boards must be steamed and boiled to remove resin and its odor, and the cardboard must also remove harmful substances such as sulfur and lime or bleaching powder. But for small trials, it is okay to use ordinary market goods, even if there is a loss, it is very small.)

Any silkworms that can go up the mountain during normal times are moved under the bottom of the box, with the silkworm's body introduced into the hole, and its tail exposed outside the bottom plate. Once half of the silkworm's body has entered the hole, it makes a cocoon in the paper roll. The excrement and leakage are all outside the bottom of the box, which can be lined with paper, making it easy to stack and not stain the lower rooms. When the silkworm spins silk, it thinks it is in the cocoon and does not see the light, so it does not turn its head, and gradually spins and retreats backward, until the silk is spun, and the pupa forms under the bottom of the box, not in the cocoon.

The procedure for collecting cocoons is very simple. Just pull the paper roll upwards and unfold it, which is more convenient than collecting cocoons on a cocoon cluster. The paper roll is still placed in the square grid for secondary use. The cycle is endless, and the cost of labor and materials saved in a year is not a small amount. And the cocoons do not need to be baked, which can avoid the disadvantages of suppression; waiting for the price to sell, there is no worry about stale cocoons, and they can be pressed and packaged, which is also more convenient for transportation.

The above plan is based on the fact that the annual production of silk floss is very large. Producing one more catty of silk floss reduces the cocoon price for silkworm farmers. The silk woven from silk floss is called cotton silk, because it is made of broken silk, which is joined into threads, so there are strands of particles floating on the silk surface, which can be stretched when pulled, which greatly reduces the price of the silk. Although it has been promoted this year to improve dyeing, and there are many users, the price is very low, and it does not benefit silkworm farmers. I want to correct this problem, and must make the silkworm pupae not in the cocoon, so that the risk of moths biting out can be avoided, so the above design is made. I sincerely hope that the financiers who are engaged in the rural lending business will adopt this new type of cocoon room, distribute it to silkworm farmers and collect their cocoons, counting by the number of cocoons instead of by the catty, then they will not change their shortsightedness and will definitely be happy to do it. (An average of 450 cocoons with pupae per catty) But by receiving one city, it is enough to change the habits of several years, and receive the benefit of a permanent solution. Foreign companies will also be happy to purchase this kind of "pupa-free cocoon," which can reduce all kinds of doubts, and the saved water and transportation costs can also be reduced by more than half.

Now is the period for autumn silkworms to go to the cocoon cluster, so make small trials to determine the plan for a large-scale implementation next spring, so that a factory can be specially built to prepare machinery to specialize in the manufacture of this product, and it can be supplied in time to help the rural economy, so that it will not be just empty talk on paper. I sincerely wish and pray for its success.

Postal Companions Entering the Pass (13) 209

— ·Qiu·Xing·Fu·Zhai·Zhu

Lu Boqin let out a sigh of relief, and took out a handkerchief to wipe the beads of sweat that shouldn't be hot but were flowing down his forehead. Tong Yizhen suddenly snatched the umbrella over, and said softly, "You should be relieved now, right? There doesn't seem to be any need to discuss other things at this time. "You're leaving in such a hurry, it's obvious that you're still angry with me. Yizhen! It's rare to go out together, can you spend half an hour more with me, and stroll around this park?" Lu Boqin was very earnest in trying to keep her.

Seeing that she was still listless, Lu Boqin didn't force her anymore, and gave her a lift: "In that case, I'm not happy to play here anymore, I'll go out with you and hire a car to take you home."

So the enthusiastic aunts and uncles could not have an open discussion with their niece.

Words

US President's Handshake Draws Blood 210

— ·Fo

In the third year of the Republic, I wrote a book called "Lectures on Boasting and Flattery" (the book was banned by Yuan Shikai not long after its publication). There is a section in it that roughly says that boasting and flattery are linked, and have positive and negative properties. For example, those who are good at boasting must like to flatter, and those who like to flatter must be good at boasting. I also cite historical facts to prove it. In fact, humans are originally materialistic animals. Assuming you see through some things, you can always see it in politics or society.

Yesterday I saw in the newspaper that when President Hoover was laying the cornerstone for the new building of the local Supreme Court, he held a reception at the White House, inviting a total of 4,000 guests. The guests were honored to shake hands with the President. About two-thirds of the 4,000 people had already shaken hands. At that time, the President's right hand was slightly broken and bleeding, probably due to being squeezed too hard. After being advised by a doctor, he retired, so the remaining guests felt disappointed. This strange situation is completely a manifestation of vanity, and this vanity is a combination of boasting and flattery.

The President is one of the people with round heads, square feet, horizontal eyes, and accurate noses, and the common people are also people with round heads, square feet, horizontal eyes, and accurate noses. We are all human beings, we are all one person. Why is a handshake an honor, and why is not shaking hands a humiliation? However, the psychology of the general guests is very different. From this, it can be seen that foreigners' vanity is richer than that of our country. Moreover, the United States is a democratic country. When the President's term expires, he becomes a commoner. Once a commoner is elected, he becomes the President. Therefore, the President and the common people are only separated by a narrow gap. Therefore, Western philosophers say that the President is the servant of the people. Since he is a servant, why is shaking hands an honor, and why is not shaking hands a humiliation?

If we extrapolate from this, then if the emperor of the autocratic era were to shake hands with a commoner, what would be the honor? I once saw a book (it was probably Suiyuan Shihua, and I can't remember the exact words, but the facts seem like this): When Emperor Shizu of the Qing Dynasty made a southern tour, the abbot of a certain monastery went out to greet him. The Emperor grabbed his arm. Since then, the monk only raised his left hand to express respect when receiving any benefactors, because his right hand had been in contact with the Emperor and would not be raised easily. I used to laugh at people in the Buddhist community for being the most materialistic and the best at flattery. If the Emperor were to stroke his beard, the monk would not eat for a long time. Originally, I said that the development of vanity was greater than that of our country, but now seeing such a situation in the United States, I can't help but sigh with admiration. But is this kind of vanity itself a bad habit, or is it an opportunity for good? I say it is an opportunity for good. Humans cannot be without this vanity. Because China lacks this vanity, we are allowed to be trampled on by others without any resistance. If there were some vanity, we would not be trampled on by foreigners like this.

Science

Natural Lacquer 212

— ·Shen·Er·Ming

Everyone knows the uses of lacquer. It is an important coating material. Ironware can be protected from rust after being lacquered, and woodenware is beautiful, durable, and most notably with natural lacquer. Therefore, I have written the general knowledge of it below.

(1) Collecting the Liquid This part of the procedure is extremely important. If you cut and slash it at will, the loss of lacquer liquid will not be small. Therefore, I will describe it first. Lacquerers often work in the mountains and proceed slowly and deliberately. Trees less than ten years old are not used. Large trees are tapped three times a year, medium trees twice, and small trees once. Each large tree yields about twenty taels of lacquer, and small trees about fifteen taels.

For wild trees, make a cut on the bark seven inches from the ground, six or seven inches long and about two tenths of an inch deep. When the lacquer is not flowing well, you can use water to moisturize it. When the lacquer is about to run out, you can place grass on the top of the tree and scorch it. Cut the tree to the roots, and the remaining lacquer will flow out from the wound.

For planted trees, make three cuts in a triangle shape, and the lacquer liquid flows out from both sides. Use a bamboo tube to hold it. Each time, a wild large tree can be cut in more than twenty places. Collect it with a bamboo tube every three hours. When the tube is full, transfer it to a lacquer bucket and cover it with hemp paper. The lacquer liquid collected at the beginning is opaque and contains water, so it needs to be purified. The method is to put the lacquer liquid in a shallow pan and expose it to the hot sun. It can be cleaned in three hours. Stir it from time to time to help the water vapor evaporate. When the whole body turns purple, use hemp cloth or cotton to clean it and store it in porcelain.

(2) Preparation Mix 1,000 parts of lacquer with 8 parts of iron filings, or 100 parts of lacquer with 5 parts of acetic acid, to get black lacquer.

Mix 128 parts of lacquer with 1 part of bone charcoal and 10 parts of cooked tea oil to get black glossy lacquer.

Mix lacquer with an equal amount of perilla oil, add water and mix well, cook to remove water, and mix with pigments to get porcelain glossy enamel.

Mix lacquer with 90 parts of cinnabar to get vermilion lacquer.

Mix lacquer with an equal amount of cooked tung oil to form a firm and glossy film. It is used to coat woodenware, does not cover the wood grain, and is resistant to moisture.

(3) Quality According to Mr. Yoshida's research, lacquer acid (Laccicacid) accounts for 85% of refined lacquer. The other 15% is colloid, brewing substance (i.e. nitrogenous body), and water. Lacquer hardens when it meets air, which is due to the action of the brewing substance. Therefore, if the brewing substance is destroyed by heat, it will not harden. Usually, the hardening time takes ten hours. Adding a small amount of glycerin only takes two hours.

Lacquer with more colloid is inferior, and lacquer with more acid is better. The most suitable temperature for drying lacquer liquid is between 10 and 30 degrees Celsius. When drying, the lacquer liquid is heavy and can increase in weight. How much it increases depends on the length of time.

Society Improvement Discussion Group

People Outside of Humans 213

— ·Tian·Fang

| How to deal with stray children on the streets |

If you are an old hand at taking streetcars in Shanghai and have a bit of experience, then you will find that there is an annoying thing: the beggars at the streetcar stops.

Yesterday morning, I was waiting for a bus at Dongxinqiao. At this time, there was a child of only six or seven years old, barefoot, with tattered clothes, holding a cigarette case in his hand, squeezing through the crowd to beg. At a young age, he had learned a mouthful of complimentary words. He followed behind the passers-by with words like "Master, young master, cultivate good fortune, get rich." At that time, a young man in a suit was walking by with a modern girl. The child spared no effort and went to nail him, following him for about dozens of steps. Finally, due to his perseverance, he received a copper coin donation. He happily jumped to the pancake stall at the intersection of Zhejiang Road across the street, combined the two copper coins originally in the box, bought a pancake, and sat on the side of the road to eat. Seeing his happy expression, even if the head of the family was eating ginseng and poria cocos cake, it would not be enough to compare. I was moved by his innocent expression at Futai, and I really felt dumbfounded. If such children were born in wealthy families, it would be the time to sit in a chartered car to go to school, but now they are wandering on the streets, running around begging for food, so that they are in contact with the bad environment every day. They are not blessed to share the material civilization of the city; but for all the evils of the city, they have long understood and learned from what they hear and see. When they grow up, how can they be asked to be good citizens?

There are probably quite a few stray children like this who are not taught or raised in Shanghai. They are educated on the streets, and they grow up in hunger and cold. What they live is an inhuman life. If they have a chance to get ahead in the future, they will only become a street thug who relies on the road to eat. This forms the vagrant class, so the society must address the root causes of eliminating vagrants and should start by taking in and educating poor and educating children, teaching them a skill so that they can become a part of production. In this way, the evils of society must be reduced a lot. This is not only creating blessings for children, but also the responsibility that those who are in charge of local administration should bear.

Among these many stray children, if they are educated, wouldn't there be one or two great heroes, but they have not been polished? Although our country has a large population, talents are buried due to the lack of universal education, which is really difficult to calculate. The people are the foundation of the country, and children are the masters of the future. Who can believe and practice these words? Ordinary people do not care about the heavy social problem, why are they not paying attention? Many wealthy people in Shanghai are afraid of being kidnapped, and they hire bodyguards at home to protect them, but they are not willing to give some relief to those who are going to do the kidnapping. It is really puzzling.

As far as I know, Shanghai has the Songhu Education and Training Institute and the Vagrant Practice Institute to take in vagrants, but neither of them is based on children. There are many inconveniences in management and education. I think we should set up a poor children's education and training institute with a large scale to take in the children of ordinary poor families, teach them ordinary knowledge - the level should be between national primary schools and civil schools, and add industrial and vocational training so that they have a skill to make a living in the future.

Educators, philanthropists, and people who care about social issues, please run one less aristocratic kindergarten, and run this paradise to create blessings for poor children! I hereby submit this idea for public discussion.

Bad Luck

金寶的厄運 214

— ·洪·水

After the Lucky Candy Store was inadvertently burned down, Jinbao also fell into terrible unemployment. Time flew by, and he spent a year in worry and sorrow! The hard-pressed life of constant distress was truly unbearable. He thought of committing suicide, if it weren't for his virtuous wife and beloved son. Now his only hope was that Xiaolian would grow up soon, start a family and career, and become a reliable support in his old age. But the reality was such: "The colder it gets, the stronger the wind blows; the poorer you are, the more likely you are to get sick." This was absolutely true; Jinbao blankly and reluctantly watched his clever and lively child, blessed with natural talent, die of illness! As a result, his wife went mad and sometimes went to the local temple to pray to the gods, hoping to ward off disaster and have a son. Now Wu Jianguang predicted that the old couple would have good luck in their old age soon; either they would build up their family business, or they would have a precious child in their old age. Therefore, they unconsciously forgot about their beloved son, Xiaolian!

Dusk grew heavy, and Jinbao's hope sank into obscurity along with the setting sun in the western mountains.

"Jinbao, will we run out of rice tomorrow?!" At the dinner table, his wife, deeply frowning, started to say to her husband in a miserable and sorrowful tone.

"Oh!" He sighed deeply, his distracted eyes looking at his wife's equally sallow and haggard face. He was afraid, and he lowered his head, as if he had a belly full of pain that he couldn't express.

"Alas! Do you want to make things even more difficult for me? Jinbao, Jinbao!"

"My dear, what do you want me to do? I'm unemployed! Didn't the fortune teller predict that I would have good luck in my old age? Don't worry for now! One day, my luck will turn, and I'll have a chance to make a fortune!"

"Heh!"

"I'm thinking of inviting a few relatives and friends to start a hui (rotating credit association) for two hundred silver dollars, to start a small business. Once it succeeds, then many problems in life won't be a problem." "What are you planning to do?"

"The freshly harvested Liangxiang chestnuts from Tianjin."

In a few days, perhaps Jinbao's good luck was about to arrive! His plan actually succeeded and was realized. He set up a chestnut stall at a corner of a bustling and crowded road, and he even publicly hung up a very eye-catching glass sign with gold lettering that read "Roadside Immortal." Jinbao, full of joy, was busy roasting chestnuts and packaging them, and he also knew that selling chestnuts required playing a phonograph to attract customers. "Farewell My Concubine," "The Fox Spirit Replacing the Prince," and "Suzhou Scenery" played non-stop in rotation. Besides donating five silver dollars to the road association and a few bags of chestnuts to the patrol officers, they generally made three or four yuan per day on average. They were so excited that they thought of the fortune teller's words and became even more overjoyed. Tonight, the stall was full of people, and business was unexpectedly booming. Jinbao, roasting chestnuts and looking at his wife, had an air of invincibility! His wife nodded and showed a smug smile, when suddenly two "uninvited guests" dressed in all black and looking fierce squeezed into the crowd. In an instant, the empty box flew into the sky, seemingly heading towards the owner who was standing there silently in a daze. The air was obviously chaotic, with shouts of "Catch, catch, catch the thieves!" Jinbao fainted next to the stove, motionless, while his wife jumped around! Their fate was thus inevitably pushed into a desperate situation.

Inconceivable.

奇怪現象 215

Strange Phenomenon 216

— ·文·炳

— ·Wen·Bing

······與一百年以前法國傅利葉監督將小麥抛棄海中事實同類······

······Similar to the fact that Fourier supervised the dumping of wheat into the sea in France a hundred years ago······

其實這種現象，並不奇怪，而且平常，古人不也說過麽，「朱門酒肉臭，路有餓死骨，」只是這純然是文學的口吻，描寫世界上的人，吃的吃不了，沒吃的餓得肚皮呌，暗示着人類生活如此不平·而沒有像社會科學那樣的加以闡明罷了。

In fact, this phenomenon is not strange, but common. Didn't the ancients also say, "Behind vermilion gates, meat and wine rot, while by the roadside, there are bones of those who died of hunger?" It's just that this is purely a literary tone, describing how some people in the world have more than they can eat, while others are so hungry that their stomachs are rumbling, implying that human life is so unequal, but it doesn't explain it in the way that social science does.

是大前天傍晚，我忽然想走到吳淞路去，於是果眞走去了，唯一的目的，自然因爲那是一條衣店馬路，天氣有些寒冷了，想去買一件起碼的絨綫衣着着，免得賤體冷壞了，喊娘喊爹！請不到醫生，住不起醫院，事實偏偏那麽捉弄人，衣店裏的定價，都與我的意思相差天遠，使我白走了一趟，慢慢地蹁到了天鐘路口，那兒正簇聚着一羣羣的呌化，灰黄色的電光，映射着他們的形相，有老婆婆，老頭兒，小孩子，衣裳是襤褸齷齷，露骨的皮肉，活像蘇詶河裏的爛泥，有的蹲着脚亂手忙，有的立在旁邊嚷呌，我知道那是無法衝進的陣圍，只好耐着性子站在近旁，等他們走散後，看到底是怎樣一回事。

The day before yesterday evening, I suddenly wanted to walk to Wusong Road, so I actually went. The only purpose, of course, was because it was a street with clothing stores. The weather was a bit cold, and I wanted to buy at least a woolen sweater to wear, so that my humble body wouldn't get cold and I wouldn't have to cry for my mom and dad! I couldn't afford a doctor or a hospital. The fact is, fate plays tricks on people. The prices in the clothing stores were so far from what I wanted, that I made a trip for nothing. I slowly staggered to the intersection of Tianzhong Road, where groups of beggars were gathered. The greyish-yellow electric light reflected their figures. There were old women, old men, and children. Their clothes were ragged and filthy, and their exposed flesh looked like the rotten mud in the Suzhou River. Some were squatting down, scrambling with their hands, while others were standing beside them, shouting. I knew that it was impossible to break into that encirclement, so I had to patiently stand nearby and wait for them to disperse before seeing what was going on.

這時候，我的腦海裏掀起了思索的旋廻，雖然猜不正那究竟是什麽一回事，但至少可以預定是與人類生活有關，尤其與低級的平民生活有關，他們不是在搶吃的食品，便是在搶爛衣及其他。　　正在沉思，他們畢竟嘩然一亂走散了，原來走來了两個紅頭阿三，手裏拿着哭喪棒，兇兇地在驅打，我走近前去，仔細端詳，那兒還殘賸着一大堆的腐爛了的黄瓜。

At this time, a whirlwind of thought arose in my mind. Although I couldn't guess exactly what was going on, I could at least predict that it was related to human life, especially to the lives of low-level commoners. They were either抢吃ing food or抢烂ing rotten clothes and other things. While I was pondering, they suddenly scattered in a chaotic rush. It turned out that two "Red-Heads" (Indian policemen) had come, holding mourning sticks in their hands and fiercely driving them away. I went closer and carefully examined the scene. There was still a large pile of rotten cucumbers left there.

黄瓜，這時候多麽可口呵！

Cucumbers, how delicious they are at this time!

在温帶，那是要夏天才有的蔬果，在夏天天然是不希奇·然一到了秋天，總算是珍貴的食品了，因爲要從南方廣東運來，在一般的食品店裏，這時候是沒有的了，（霞飛路一帶的食品店中，自然陳列多着·）雖然一般人所需要的還是麵包，沒有口福去嘗試這過時佳品的滋味，但該當如何的珍視它！而今竟把它腐爛，抛棄，這是何等奇怪的務盾現象！

In the temperate zone, cucumbers are vegetables and fruits that are only available in summer. In summer, they are naturally not rare. However, once autumn arrives, they are considered precious foods because they have to be transported from Guangdong in the south. In general food stores, they are not available at this time (naturally, there are many on display in food stores around Avenue Joffre). Although what ordinary people need is still bread, and they don't have the good fortune to try the taste of this out-of-season delicacy, how much should they cherish it! Yet now it is rotten and discarded. What a strange and contradictory phenomenon!

我思忖過後，與頭一望，原來就在XX蔬果行的店前，那兒的玻璃裏還陳列着各種貴重的新鮮食品，更使我憶起一百年以前法國一件同類，意義尤較重大的事實。

After thinking it over, I looked up and saw that it was right in front of the XX fruit and vegetable store. Various valuable and fresh foods were still on display in the glass window, which made me recall a similar, even more significant, event in France a hundred years ago.

那是如此的；

It was like this:

大約離今一百年前，法國有一人名呌傅利葉，他年幼時在馬賽一個糧食店裏工作，有一天那糧食店裏要將從停泊馬賽港的船舶輸入的小麥抛棄到海裏去，他受命去做這事的監督，當時法國正遇着凶荒，缺少小麥，多數窮人，都以馬鈴，薯代麵包吃，可是那些糧食商人，却還爲着抬高小麥價錢，將輸入的小麥匿藏船裏，以致小麥腐爛，着人抛棄海中，一方面有多數要小麥而無小麥可吃的人，他方面又有特意將輸入的小麥使其腐爛而棄海裏的人·這究竟是什麽一回事呢？傅利葉看見這種奇怪的現象，就起了一個欵問·以爲現在的社會組織，一定有了什麽缺陷，從此以後，他就犧牲他一生去研究理想社會的組織。　　其實這是很平常的事實，只是於今爲烈，我們該怎樣去應付這矛盾現象呵

About a hundred years ago, there was a man in France named Fourier. When he was young, he worked in a grain store in Marseille. One day, the grain store was going to dump wheat imported from ships docked in the port of Marseille into the sea. He was ordered to supervise this matter. At that time, France was experiencing a famine and was short of wheat. Most poor people ate potatoes instead of bread, but the grain merchants were still hiding the imported wheat in ships to raise the price of wheat, causing the wheat to rot and ordering people to dump it into the sea. On the one hand, there were many people who wanted wheat but had no wheat to eat, and on the other hand, there were people who deliberately caused the imported wheat to rot and dumped it into the sea. What exactly was going on? When Fourier saw this strange phenomenon, he had a question. He believed that there must be some flaws in the current social organization. From then on, he sacrificed his life to study the organization of an ideal society. In fact, this is a very common fact, but it is even more intense today. How should we deal with this contradictory phenomenon?

刑事第二審判决沈福田濫發支票提起上訴案原判决關於沈福田罪刑部分撤銷沈福田無罪

Criminal Second Instance Judgment: Shen Futian filed an appeal for issuing bad checks. The original judgment regarding Shen Futian's crime and penalty is revoked. Shen Futian is innocent.

民事第一審判决王品三與程修齡欠欵及確認優先處償權案（主文）程懷德黨應支付原告之借欵五百元及自民國十七年二月十四日起至執行終了日止按月一分五厘利息被告應負清理償還之責前項金額原告就抵押物之賣得假金有優先處償權訴訟費用由被告負担源安輪船公司與上海中威輪船公司解約案（主文）被竺應償還原告洋三千八百零零八角一分原告其餘之訴駁回訴訟費用由被告負担三分之二餘由原告負担奚鄒氏與鄒順發析産案（主文）被告應將坐落上邑二十三保十二圖臣字圩二百零九號則田一畝六分溝水單二分宅基四分屋六間二十三保九圓截墳地一畝與原告平均分析原告其餘之訴駁回訴訟費用由被告負担七分之六餘由原告負担泰興麵粉號與王福興貨欵案（主文）被告應償還原告貨欵三百七十八元八角七分並自民國二十一年九月一日起至執行終了日止常年五厘之遲延利息其餘之訴駁回訴訟費用由被告負担陳鶴松與張心銘等借欵案（主文）被告張心銘應償還原告借欵洋一百元及自民國十五年二月十九日起至執行終了日止常年二分利息如張心銘不履行債務時由被告崔松琴代償其餘之訴駁回訴訟費用由被告張心銘負担所簿生與劉國藩等借欵案（主文）被告劉國藩應償還原告借欵五百元如其財産經强制執行而無效果時應由被告劉二保代償四百元被告劉順華代償一百元訴訟費用由被告劉國藩負担粤商酒樓與陳耀庭等欠欵案（主文）被告陳耀庭應償還原告欠欵二百四十六元被告利興號應償還原告房租五十九元被告鄒貴生應償還原告欠欵一百零一元四角八分訴訟費用由被告比例負担義興錢莊與范壽臣賠償案（主文）被告償還原告洋九萬二千九百五十七元並自起訴日起至執行終了日止週年百分之五之法定利息訴訟費用由被告負担張子遠與劉裕良貨欵案（主文）被告應償還原告貨欵銀八十七元七角一分訴訟費用由被告負担

Civil First Instance Judgment in the case of Wang Pin-san versus Cheng Xiu-ling for debt and confirmation of priority of repayment (Main Text): Cheng Huai-de Party shall pay the plaintiff's loan of 500 yuan and interest at 1.5% per month from February 14, 1928, until the end of execution. The defendant shall be responsible for cleaning up and repaying the debt. The plaintiff has priority of repayment for the aforementioned amount from the proceeds of the sale of the mortgaged property. The costs of the lawsuit shall be borne by the defendant. Case of Yuan An Shipping Company versus Shanghai Zhongwei Shipping Company for contract termination (Main Text): The defendant should repay the plaintiff 3,800 yuan, 8 jiao, and 1 fen. The plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected. Two-thirds of the lawsuit costs shall be borne by the defendant and the remainder by the plaintiff. Case of Xi Zhou-shi versus Zhou Shun-fa for property division (Main Text): The defendant should divide with the plaintiff the following property located at No. 209, Chenziwei, Tuchen Map, Section 12, Bao 23, Shangyi: 1.6 mu of paddy field, 0.2 mu of ditch water, 0.4 mu of homestead, six rooms, and 1 mu of burial ground at No. 9, Yuanduan, Bao 23, equally. The plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected. Six-sevenths of the lawsuit costs shall be borne by the defendant and the remainder by the plaintiff. Case of Taixing Flour Store versus Wang Fuxing for payment of goods (Main Text): The defendant should repay the plaintiff's debt of 378 yuan, 8 jiao, and 7 fen, and annual 5% default interest from September 1, 1932, until the end of execution. The remaining claims are rejected. The costs of the lawsuit shall be borne by the defendant. Case of Chen He-song versus Zhang Xin-ming and others for loans (Main Text): The defendant Zhang Xin-ming should repay the plaintiff's loan of 100 yuan and annual 2% interest from February 19, 1926, until the end of execution. If Zhang Xin-ming fails to fulfill the debt, the defendant Cui Song-qin shall repay it on his behalf. The remaining claims are rejected. The costs of the lawsuit shall be borne by the defendant Zhang Xin-ming. Case of Suo Bo-sheng versus Liu Guo-fan and others for loans (Main Text): The defendant Liu Guo-fan should repay the plaintiff's loan of 500 yuan. If his property is forcibly executed and there is no effect, the defendant Liu Er-bao shall repay 400 yuan on his behalf, and the defendant Liu Shun-hua shall repay 100 yuan. The costs of the lawsuit shall be borne by the defendant Liu Guo-fan. Case of Yue Shang Restaurant versus Chen Yao-ting and others for debt (Main Text): The defendant Chen Yao-ting should repay the plaintiff's debt of 246 yuan. The defendant Lixing Store should repay the plaintiff's rent of 59 yuan. The defendant Zou Gui-sheng should repay the plaintiff's debt of 101 yuan, 4 jiao, and 8 fen. The costs of the lawsuit shall be borne by the defendants proportionally. Case of Yi Xing Money Shop versus Fan Shou-chen for compensation (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 92,957 yuan and the statutory interest of 5% per annum from the date of filing the lawsuit until the end of execution. The costs of the lawsuit shall be borne by the defendant. Case of Zhang Zi-yuan versus Liu Yu-liang for payment of goods (Main Text): The defendant should repay the plaintiff's debt of silver 87 yuan, 7 jiao, and 1 fen. The costs of the lawsuit shall be borne by the defendant.

民事批示葉莊氏爲與葉少初離異案聲請執行由狀悉查此案卷宗尙未奉上級審發還所請暫從緩議此批勞本生爲與亞琴台太司欠租安請追償尾數由狀悉查債務人另案並無餘欵存案仰候續傅追繳可也此批阿特生爲與凌阿元欠欵請領銀洋由狀悉查債務人尙未將欵交案巳傅保勒交矣此批曹元財爲與董兆森賠償案聲請執行由狀悉據債務人交洋一百零五元餘巳傅保追繳矣此批阿木生爲與孫阿海等欠欵案聲請查封由狀悉准予派員查封此批俞福鑫限定繼承聲請展期呈報由狀悉准予展期三月此批祥盛米號爲與黄順興等欠欵案聲請執行由狀悉案巳上訴所請應從緩議此批羅傑經租處爲與商溪旅館欠租聲請啟封銷案由狀悉應准啟封銷案此批鮑温爲與高子白保證債務案聲請銷案由狀悉應准銷案此批孫維範爲與周逹甫欠租案請傅原告勸令減輕拔還由狀悉候傅案訊奪此批唐贊元爲與王金生欠租安聲請併案執行由狀悉准予併安執行此批
